Important Telegrams Two

Outline of Political Reorganization in Hubei Province 16

Announced by Commander-in-Chief Chiang at a Party and Government Meeting

(Hankou) Commander-in-Chief Chiang, in order to reorganize the political situation in Hubei, has formulated an eighteen-point outline for the reorganization of Hubei's political affairs. Among these points, some important policies are already underway, some are just beginning, and some are still in the planning stages. The outline was announced at a recent party and government meeting, and the full text is as follows: (1) Implement the system of Administrative Commissioners to ensure that they can fully exercise their powers. (2) Be cautious in selecting county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs. Their performance should be thoroughly assessed and guaranteed, and regulations on rewards and punishments should be strictly enforced. (3) The existing police forces and local self-defense security teams in each county should be strictly reorganized, their structures improved, their numbers verified, their funding sources determined, and their publicly or privately owned firearms should be secured. They should be thoroughly trained, with special emphasis on political common sense and martial arts. (4) After the reorganization of the security teams and other local self-defense groups in each county, the terms of service for able-bodied men in each county should be stipulated as regular, reserve, and backup, without dividing areas of jurisdiction. Internal administration will be guided by military orders. The Security Department will draft implementation plans and proceed in stages. The first phase of reorganization should be completed by March of the 22nd year [1933]. (5) Implement the household registration and Bao-Jia system in accordance with the relevant regulations, and complete the household registration within the prescribed time limit. In special circumstances where it is genuinely impossible to complete the registration on time, a request can be submitted for an extension, but the deadline must not exceed March of the 22nd year [1933]. The entire province must complete the registration uniformly, and a complete review of the entire province should be conducted from May to September of the same year. (6) Except for the budgets of the Hubei Provincial Government and the Hankou Municipal Government, which have already been approved, the revenue and expenditure of all local finances of all county governments and their subordinate agencies throughout the province should be compiled into formal budgets and submitted to the Department of Finance for approval and implementation. From February of next year [1933], all expenditures must be implemented in accordance with the budget. (7) The establishment of the Provincial Farmers' Bank and the credit cooperatives in each county should be preliminarily completed by March of the 22nd year [1933]. (8) The land survey is scheduled to be completed in five years, but the preliminary plan for the first year of the 22nd year [1933] should be specified as soon as possible. (9) All financial institutions should immediately implement an accounting system. (10) All levels of financial personnel must obtain guarantees, and the主管 authorities should supervise them at any time. If there are any cases of embezzlement or fraud, compensation should be pursued and legal punishments enforced. (11) The provincial highway construction plan will be drafted by the Department of Construction, and the road construction will be carried out in phases within one year. The first phase of work should be completed by March of the 22nd year [1933]. (12) Hubei's embankment and water conservancy projects should be transferred to the overall planning of the National Economic Council, and the Jianghan Engineering Bureau under the council should be held responsible for handling the projects, in order to save resources and prevent abuses. (13) In the counties of Hubei, especially in the areas affected by bandits, in addition to working hard to restore the rural areas in accordance with the Land Handling Regulations and the Rural Cooperative Regulations, appropriate areas should be selected to establish group farms to experiment with new farming and management methods. (14) In elementary and secondary education, students should be encouraged to develop a sense of national identity and cultivate a spirit of sacrifice for the country in all courses. (15) Elementary and junior high schools should actively train Boy Scouts. (16) Schools above the junior high level should emphasize military education and make students' lives militarized. (17) The Department of Education will formulate a one-year plan for the literacy movement for the common people, starting from Wuhan. (18) All levels of judicial organs should clear up backlog cases within a limited time. Civil and criminal lawsuits should be concluded within a maximum of one month in accordance with the established procedures, so as to avoid the people suffering from litigation. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 18th)

Zeng Zhongming Discusses Road Construction 17

The Shao-Le Section of the Yuehan Railway and the Tong-Hua Section of the Longhai Railway

The Roadbed Work is Largely Completed

The Taitong Branch Line has Already Been Surveyed

(Nanjing) Zeng Zhongming, Vice Minister of Railways, discussed the recent developments in road construction as follows:

(1) The Guangzhou-Shaozhou and Wuchang-Zhuzhou sections of the Yuehan Railway have long been completed and opened to traffic. The Zhuzhou-Shaozhou section, which is currently under construction, is 435 kilometers long. In the area where Hunan and Guangdong provinces meet, it is necessary to pass through the highest mountain range, which is the watershed between the Yangtze River and the Pearl River. The route must pass through this area, and the construction is extremely difficult. The route of this section has been largely determined. As for the Shaozhou-Lechang section, which is about 50 kilometers long, the roadbed work has been largely completed. As long as the funds are allocated, the Shao-Le section can be opened to traffic first in a few months. The route north of Lechang can also be started. It is estimated that the construction cost of the entire Lechang-Zhuzhou section will be more than 70 million yuan. It has been decided to use two-thirds of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity as the construction fund for this project. The audit shows that the total amount is almost the same. However, this kind of fund is returned in installments every year until the 45th year of the Republic [1956] before it can be fully paid. In order to cope with the rapid completion of the Yuehan Railway, it is planned to consult with the board of directors managing the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity to borrow the future installments as a fund to issue public bonds. Detailed plans are currently being drafted and discussed.

(2) The Longhai Railway spans four provinces: Gansu, Shaanxi, Henan, and Jiangsu, and is 1,600 li long. It is an important artery for the development of the Northwest. The route built before the 16th year of the Republic [1927] was from Haizhou Dapu in Jiangsu to Lingbao in Hebei, about 825 kilometers long. Now, the 72-kilometer-long route west of Lingbao to Tongguan has been continuously built and completed, and traffic has started since December 18 of last year. The 130-kilometer-long section from Tongguan to Xi'an, of which 24 kilometers from Tongguan to Huayin, has also been largely completed. The eastern end of the railway was temporarily located at Haizhou Dapu. Now, because the Honghe estuary is silted up and the Dapu wharf has lost its effectiveness, the eastern end of the route has been extended to Shiyao on the opposite bank of the Xilian Island, and a temporary wharf is being built there to facilitate land and water transportation. This project is currently being tendered separately and should be completed in a few months.

(3) The Taitong Branch Line. The Shandong Zhongxing Coal Mining Company is a well-known coal mine in China. The Taitao Railway, a special railway built by the company from Taierzhuang to Zaozhuang near the mine, cannot fully transport coal from Zaozhuang to the Lincheng Station of the Jinpu Railway. Now that we are advocating the development of our country's coal production, we should try our best to find a way, so it is determined to build a railway from Taierzhuang to Tonghe Station of the Longhai Railway.

(4) The Capital Ferry. A special ferry ordered from England has been launched in England and will soon be shipped to China. All the machinery on the wharves has been ordered from abroad. The construction of the local platforms on both sides started in December of the 19th year [1930], and it is expected that traffic will be open in the summer of next year. In the future, the Shanghai-Pingpu through train will only take 47 or 48 hours to reach.

In addition, teams have been sent to survey the Yue-Dian, Xiang-Dian, Jing-Yue, and Qin-Yu lines, but due to the situation, only a section has been surveyed and not completed. The survey work for the Jing-Xiang and Bao-Ning lines has been completed long ago, and construction will start as soon as the funds are raised. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

Rumors of Lu Dipin's Death Denied 18

His Condition is Improving, and He is Able to Go Out

The Secretary-General of the Provincial Government Sends a Corrective Telegram

Doctor Lu Wenzhao Discusses the Course of Treatment

(Hangzhou) It is not true that Chairman Lu has passed away. At 4 p.m. today, Lu walked to the Provincial Government and had dinner at the branch of Zhou's office in No. 31, You Sheng Jin Lane. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

(Hangzhou) Lu Wenzhao, director of the Department of Diagnosis and Treatment of the Shanghai Red Cross Hospital, made a statement tonight at 8 p.m. about the treatment of Chairman Lu, saying that he was summoned by Chairman Lu to Hangzhou for consultation and arrived in Hangzhou on the 7th and stayed at the Provincial Government. He diagnosed that Chairman Lu was suffering from a mild stroke, and the only nerves affected were the left internal and left tongue nerves. The left foot was slightly weak and difficult to walk, but his mind was clear and his speech was normal. His stomach was also strong. After taking medicine and resting, his condition improved day by day. In recent days, his pulse was 66 to 74, and his body temperature was 36.4 to 37 degrees. Everything was normal. Chairman Lu has a strong sense of responsibility. He personally reviewed all important documents and browsed all the newspapers in this port, as well as in Shanghai, Tianjin, Nanjing, Hankou, Hunan, and Jiangxi. Today, all the newspapers in Shanghai reported that Lu was unable to get up. Where did the rumors come from? It is very strange. I hereby reveal the current situation so that those who care about Chairman Lu can understand the truth. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

(Hangzhou) Lu Dai, Secretary-General of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, issued a telegram saying that all newspaper offices were shocked by the news of Chairman Lu's death in the Shanghai newspapers today. Chairman Lu previously suffered from cerebral congestion and was treated by Dr. Lu Wenzhao. His condition has improved day by day, and his diet is as usual. He needs about a few weeks of recuperation to fully recover. The rumors from the outside are all nonsense. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

(Beiping) Yesterday, the newspapers in Pingjin reported that Lu Dipin died of a stroke on the 16th. His younger brother, Dangping, sent a telegram to Lu Lushan, Secretary-General of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, to inquire. According to the reply telegram, Lu Dipin's condition has improved, proving that the death rumor is not true. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

Steel Plant Contract Awaits Approval by the Legislative Yuan 22

The Plant Site Has Not Yet Been Determined

(Nanjing) Huang Jintao of the Mining Department of the Ministry of Industry said that the content of the steel plant contract will soon be submitted to the Executive Yuan for transfer to the Legislative Yuan for review and approval before it can be signed. It is expected that coal will be produced in one and a half years and steel will be produced in three years. However, the plant site has not yet been determined. From an economic point of view, the plant site should be located in Pukou, because the products can be directly loaded onto ships from the dock, which reduces the cost and can compete with foreign goods. If national defense is emphasized, the cost will be higher and it will not be able to compete with foreign goods. As a result, the plant we run ourselves is equivalent to not running it. Therefore, the plant site is very important and must be decided recently. The factory borrowed 10 million US dollars from the German company Xiwang. All the procedures of the contract have been negotiated. The internal organization of the steel plant is divided into nine departments: steelmaking, general affairs, technology, engineering, business, audit, and accounting. Each department is divided into two or three sections. The plant has one director, and each department and section has one director and section chief. The total number of workers is about 2,000. In order to prevent the director from abusing his power, the Ministry of Industry intends to make the audit and accounting departments independent and not subject to the director's control, and the ministry will directly supervise the accounts. The selection of the director and other personnel will also be submitted by the Ministry of Industry to the Central Government for appointment to show solemnity. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

Ministry of Finance Investigates the Amount of Refined Salt Shipped to Shanghai from Liaoning Province 36

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has found that a large amount of refined salt produced by the Liaoning District Liyuan, Fengtian, Fuhai, Laihua, Hongyuan, and Huafeng refined salt companies has been shipped to Shanghai this year, and some has also been shipped to Tianjin for sale. Some coarse salt has been disguised as refined salt. In addition to the fact that shipping to Tianjin for transshipment violates Article 34 of the Refined Salt Regulations, which is being investigated, the Salt Affairs Audit General Office has been ordered to instruct the Songjiang branch to find out how much refined salt each refined salt company in the Liaoning district has shipped to Shanghai this year. If any exceeds the approved maximum amount, it will be investigated and prohibited, and the shipped salt will be sealed and sales will be stopped. If there are new companies in the Liaoning district that have shipped refined salt in addition to the above six companies, they will be investigated and confiscated to maintain the salt administration. A list of the amount of refined salt shipped to Shanghai by each refined salt company in the Liaoning district from January to now will be submitted, and monthly reports will be submitted thereafter for evaluation. (Special dispatch on the 18th)

Important Foreign Telegrams 47

After the Resignation of the Papen Cabinet, Hindenburg Consults with Party Leaders on Forming a National Coalition Government, Hitler Insists on the National Socialist Party Forming the Cabinet

▲National Press Agency, Berlin, 17th - The German Papen Cabinet resigned to the President today. After accepting the resignation, the President ordered them to continue to handle political affairs as usual while he consulted with party leaders on whether to form a national coalition cabinet. He also instructed party leaders to stay in Beijing over the weekend to discuss the issue of a successor cabinet. Subsequently, the Presidential Palace announced that the President would meet with Center Party leader Kaas and National People's Party leader Hugenberg on Friday, and then meet with People's Party leader Tingeltai that evening. On Saturday, he would meet with National Socialist Party leader Hitler and Bavarian People's Party leader Scheffer for discussions.

▲Reuters, Munich, 18th - According to Hitler's headquarters here, Hitler is unlikely to participate in President Hindenburg's consultations with party leaders on Saturday. He continues to insist on his previous declaration that the National Socialist Party must lead the government, otherwise he would prefer to stay out of it. He is preparing to gain full control at that time.

▲Reuters, Berlin, 18th - President Hindenburg has been meeting with party leaders since this morning, but whether there are any new developments in the political situation is being kept secret. Whether the organization of a national unity government is possible depends on Hitler's meeting with the President tomorrow. If the National Socialist Party leader insists on obtaining the position of Chancellor, the hope of a national unity government will be dashed. At the same time, Hitler's close friends are advising him to accept important positions in the new cabinet that the President can offer. All newspapers believe that the new cabinet will not be very different from the old cabinet. The position of Minister of Defense will still belong to Schleicher, and Neurath will still be in charge of Foreign Affairs.

▲National Press Agency, Berlin, 17th - It is now believed that the success of a coalition cabinet depends on Hitler's attitude. However, Hitler is not yet willing to express his opinion, saying that he is preparing a written opinion to present to the President on Saturday. At this time, he can only declare that he opposes the Papen Cabinet's economic plan. Furthermore, the Social Democratic Party has already issued a letter with strong wording, declaring its refusal to discuss the issue of forming a talent-centered cabinet with the President. As for Berlin at this time, the people are calm, and it is rumored that the President has authorized Papen to continue to act indefinitely, so there should not be a period of chaos that traps the central government in a leaderless situation.

Reasons for Papen's Announcement of Resignation 48

When the Papen Cabinet resigned to the President, it issued a communique announcing the circumstances of its contacts with party leaders in recent days in an attempt to follow the President's wishes in organizing a coalition cabinet. It said that Papen had talked with various parties and hoped to form a cabinet with a very broad base. Unfortunately, there were no results. Although the National People's Party and the Bavarian People's Party welcomed any coalition cabinet as long as it could guide the country to resolve the current difficult situation, the Center Party indicated that under the leadership of the current cabinet leader, it may not be sufficiently strong to resolve the difficulties. The Social Democratic Party refused outright, and the National Socialist Party only agreed to continue negotiations in writing and would submit a memorandum opposing the current government's economic policy. It also said that the cabinet, given the difficulties of the situation, had been trying its best to seek the greatest welfare of the motherland since it accepted the important task entrusted by the President on July 1. Finally, it said that it has now returned its powers to the President. At this time of hardship, it cannot make any further personal plans, so the cabinet withdraws, allowing the President to freely gather the national strength in the position of national leader to solve the current crisis, and so on.

Confused Political Situation 49

▲Reuter, Berlin, 17th. The German political situation has become greatly turbulent. It is expected that the President will instruct the Minister of Defence, Schleicher, to form a cabinet. This could lead to a military dictatorship by Dikt. Before resigning, Papen received a letter from the National Socialist Party leader, Hitler, the contents of which have not been announced. However, it is rumored that Hitler is demanding to be appointed as Prime Minister as a condition for the National Socialist Party to join the government. President Hindenburg is said to strongly oppose this. President Kubon of the United States is also rumored to be a successor to the Prime Minister. However, Mr. Kubon may not be able to obtain more parliamentary support than Papen. If each party does not agree to form a national centralized or extra-party cabinet, the President may still instruct the current executive to continue. If so, the parliament will inevitably vote against it, and the question of how to avoid violating the constitution will arise. A National Socialist Party newspaper stated that Hitler is demanding the position of Prime Minister. Currently, a government that can occupy a majority in parliament must be formed by a combination of the National Socialist Party, the Centre Party, and the German National People's Party. However, the political views of these parties are fundamentally different. Observers of the political situation predict that Papen will become a dictator, but it is difficult to predict what will happen afterwards. Various sectors in Germany are very concerned about the current situation.

▲National News Agency, Berlin, 18th. The sudden resignation of the Papen cabinet has caused great shock, but the capital city appears to be very calm, and the national order has not been disturbed. According to various sources close to the President, the President has not yet made a decision on the candidate for the next Prime Minister. However, a powerful faction in the political circles believes that this position will be given to Hitler, with the agreement that the cabinet he organizes will be independent of the parliament but will still need the support of the parliament to resolve important issues. Other political observers say that no party leader has any hope of forming a cabinet at this time. It is expected that the President will entrust state affairs to someone with political experience and somewhat neutral. This kind of cabinet will recruit members from several political parties and be able to obtain the support of each party in the parliament when the time is right. Therefore, Dr. Barlach, who has been acting as a Prussian state affairs commissioner since July 20, special management commissioner Goerdeler, former Minister of Defence Dr. Geissler, former colonial governor Dr. Schnee (i.e., the German member of the League of Nations investigation team for the Sino-Japanese dispute), and current Minister of Defence General Schleicher have the highest voices. However, any such cabinet depends on the support of the National Socialist Party in the parliament. Otherwise, the National Socialist Party can propose a vote of no confidence at any time and obtain the support of the Communist Party to overturn it. The two parties occupy 296 seats in the 585-seat parliament. In short, the overall situation is very dangerous now, and the first decision is entirely in the hands of President Hindenburg.

Major Powers Express Their Attitudes at the Disarmament Conference 50

Britain Agrees to Establish a Permanent Disarmament Committee

US Representative Willing to Continue Cooperation in Geneva

France Agrees to Fully Consider British Disarmament Proposals

▲Reuter, Geneva, 17th. British Foreign Secretary Simon stated in a speech to the main body of the Disarmament Conference today that Germany's request to reorganize its combat troops should be managed under a set of reorganization conditions and implemented in a way that does not contradict any arms limitations or reductions, and must not contain an increase in military aggression. The Foreign Secretary continued to say that the British government is deeply moved by President Hoover's proposals regarding the strength of the military and is prepared to accept them as the basis for discussion. The British government also accepts in principle the resolution passed by the Disarmament Conference on June 22 to establish a permanent disarmament committee, believing that the stipulation of effective supervision is essential for negotiating a disarmament convention. The Foreign Secretary also turned to Chairman Henderson and said, "We have reached a turning point in this conference. It is useless to engage in the details of the disarmament machinery without the spirit of peace. We are now working to consolidate international goodwill." The Italian representative strongly supported the disarmament proposals put forward by Foreign Secretary Simon, but said that if Germany is absent, these problems cannot be solved. US Representative Davis said that the Disarmament Conference has been meeting for ten months, and economic misfortunes are increasing. However, if there is a glimmer of hope for success, the US delegation is willing to continue working in Geneva. The French representative said that the British proposals will receive France's full consideration. The French representative reiterated the French policy previously stated by French Minister of War Peng Gu, and then briefly described France's disarmament plan.

▲Reuter, Tokyo, 18th. The Japanese political circles do not want to lightly comment on British Foreign Secretary Simon's disarmament speech before it is formally verified. However, the general impression is very good, especially for the Navy Department. According to a spokesman from the department, Simon's proposal on installing smaller artillery positions on battleships is in line with Japan's views. The spokesman also said that Japan advocates abolishing aircraft carriers but cannot agree to abolish submarines.

Japanese Government Publishes Opinion on the League of Nations 57

Doing Its Utmost to Denigrate China

What Is Said Is Nothing More Than the Old Tune of the Japanese

▲Den Tsushin, Tokyo, 18th. The revised points of the Japanese government's opinion on the Lytton Report have been completely finalized. The original has arrived at the Japanese delegation in Geneva, and the procedures for submitting it to the League of Nations Secretariat have been completed. The outline of the opinion has been released by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today, as follows:

Introduction: The Japanese are satisfied with the following two points in the Lytton Report: (1) It recognizes the fact that China is divided and chaotic and in a state of anarchy. (2) It recognizes that China's boycott of Japanese goods is encouraged and sponsored by the Nanjing government and is carried out by illegal means and violence. However, the judgment is made under evidence that is unfavorable to Japan and favorable to China. From the beginning of the dispatch of the Lytton Committee, it has held a priori subjective idea that the army of one country is invading foreign territory. What appropriate method is used to correct this, so that such an illegal conclusion can be obtained? The committee members may not understand Chinese and stayed for a short period of time, which may be one of the reasons.

Chapter 1: China. Although China is a country that was once unified and exists, it is now just a name for a vast region. However, although China is in a state of disunity and anarchy, Europeans and Americans cannot remove the concept of it existing as a country. The principle of territorial inviolability is sacred, but it can be applied to a country in a state of anarchy that is no longer a country. After the collapse of the last government that unified China, Yuan Shikai's republican government, China had no government existence, and the existence of the country also ceased at the same time. The agreement of the Washington Conference to recognize the existence of a unified government in China is the cause of China's decline. China is just a hope and an ideal, not a country at all. The countries only recognize the Nanjing government within the scope of its authority. Manchuria is naturally not within its scope. Even the Lytton Report does not recognize that Manchuria is under the command of the Nanjing government.

Chapter 2: Manchuria. Manchuria initially existed independently of the mainland of China. Although it was temporarily merged when the Qing Dynasty was established, it naturally separated after the Qing Dynasty died. The two generations of the Zhang family were not subject to any restraint from the mainland of China. In 1928, although Zhang Xueliang had some contact with the Nanjing government, the opportunity for independence naturally brewed among the people of Manchuria due to the tyranny of the two generations of the Zhang family.

Chapter 3: The September 18th Incident and Subsequent Military Actions. Although the committee recognizes the railway bombing, it does not say who did it. It also determines that the actions of the Japanese army exceeded the scope of self-defense. However, if Japan had taken emergency measures at that time, Japan would have been expelled from Manchuria. The committee's determination is biased towards China's explanation and does not know that the emergency situation between China and Japan is the result of the continuous aggressive attitude of China. The committee is indifferent to this level. It also says that the bombing of Jinzhou was inappropriate. Japan's actions were legitimate actions recognized by the Hague Convention.

Chapter 4: "New Country". The report seems to determine that the "new country" was created by the Japanese army, but it turns a blind eye to the fact that the Japanese government and military headquarters have strictly ordered that no Japanese, even individuals, are allowed to participate in the Manchurian political movement. The report also determines that the residents of Manchuria do not want to be under Japanese rule, but this cannot be interpreted as hoping to restore a state of anarchy and the rule of the Nanjing government. If the residents of Manchuria hope for the restoration of the Zhang regime, why was the Zhang regime expelled from Manchuria? The committee's determination that Japan created "Manchukuo" has not been carefully examined in this regard. The report recognizes that such a result exists under the presence of foreign troops, but this is limited to when foreign troops are hostile. For example, the Estonian revolution was carried out with the assistance of the US Navy, but it was immediately recognized. In short, "Manchukuo" is ruled by the Manchus, and even the Chinese welcome it because they can be stable.

Chapter 5: Conclusion. Chapters 9 and 10 of the report are based on the above-mentioned errors. In particular, the establishment of "Manchukuo" and the investigation by the investigation committee have changed the situation at that time, so the instructions have no value for solving the problem. Based on the above reasons, it is believed that the fundamental solution to the Sino-Japanese dispute requires the correct understanding of the reality of China and Manchuria by the countries and the nurturing of "Manchukuo" in order to maintain lasting peace in the Far East and world peace.

The gist of the Japanese government's opinion is nothing more than (1) slandering China as not being a country, (2) recognizing that Manchuria has no relationship with China, (3) the so-called new country was not created by Japan, and (4) accusing the League of Nations report of insufficient understanding. These kinds of absurd and irrational fallacies that ignore facts and disregard justice have long been extensively publicized, and this newspaper has repeatedly refuted them in articles, so there is no value in debating them again. However, today it is actually using this kind of extremely unreasonable and absurd fallacy to form the official documents of the League of Nations. The denunciation of our country not only does not slightly take into account international etiquette, but also uses fabrication to the fullest extent, no different from a rogue cursing. Instead of reflecting on its own internal disturbances and incessant assassinations and mergers, it boasts to be better than our country. It is so inconsiderate and unrestrained. This is what is called unbearable! How can it not make our people more outraged? As for its conclusion that the facts of Manchuria and China should be recognized to maintain peace in the Far East, we dare to ask the League of Nations: If the League of Nations can indeed abolish the Covenant and the Nine-Power Treaty and the Non-War Treaty, then it can recognize what it calls the current facts. If it cannot, what reason will it have to recognize its facts? League of Nations members, please think carefully.

Roosevelt Expresses Political Views on War Debts 59

Hoover Agreed to Meet at the White House Next Week by Phone

Hoover Will Also Convene Congressional Leaders to Discuss Together

Democratic Policy Based on the Principle of "One With One Take"

Reducing Tariffs as an Essential Plan for the International Economy to Recover

▲National News Agency, Albany, 17th. Roosevelt reported to President Hoover in person on the phone today that he was prepared to arrive in Beijing at 3:45 pm next Tuesday and go to the White House to meet him, and expressed his eagerness to cooperate. After Mr. Roosevelt decided to enter Beijing, he would publish a part of his foreign policy, believing that high tariffs and foreign debts were interrelated. If tariffs could be reduced together, trade could be promoted and the debtor countries could also have the strength to repay foreign debts. He believed that the international policy of the Democratic government should be based on "one with one take" to exchange benefits with other countries, believing that there are many interests that one country can exchange with another, and the result can at least limit the damage to its own interests. Unfortunately, everyone has ignored them now. Reducing tariffs is the first priority of this policy and an essential plan for the international economy to start on the road to recovery. If foreign countries can sell their goods, they can also buy goods and have the surplus to repay debts. He also said that he would convene a special meeting of Congress after taking office, at which time he would publish his entire policy.

Opposition in Parliament 60

▲National News Agency, Washington, 17th. Since Roosevelt accepted the invitation and scheduled to enter Beijing, neutral observers now believe that the two presidents will be able to agree with the leaders of the two parties on a plan that can be accepted by Congress. Hoover and Roosevelt will probably start discussing on Tuesday night, and if the two can agree on the war debt issue, they will convene congressional leaders the next day to propose suggestions for joint discussion. It is heard that Hoover has summoned three Republican leaders of the Senate Finance Committee, Smots, Watson, and Reed, to meet on Wednesday. At that time, three Republican leaders of the House Ways and Means Committee, Halle and others, will also participate, and their purpose is to solicit opinions from Congress on the extension of the suspension period and proposals, and on how to raise money to offset the debts due next month after the debtor countries suspend payments.

▲Reuter, Washington, 17th. House Democratic Leader Reni said today that any proposal to extend the repayment period of European war debts owed to the United States will not be easy to gain the support of the House. The general opinion of the House and its leaders can be seen. House Foreign Affairs Committee Chairman Linoz also said that the House does not approve of any changes to the existing agreement. Another important figure in the Democratic Party, McFatty Light, also opposes modifying war debts, saying that President Hoover's deferred payment plan failed in the national vote and that he could not continue to follow this, so he does not want to propose another extension.

▲Reuter, Washington, 17th. Republican Congressman Sheridan declared today that if the major European countries do not pay the debts due to the United States in mid-December, he will submit a resolution ordering the announcement that each country is unable to repay the debt and has entered bankruptcy, so it cannot be responsible for international trade and diplomacy. It is said that if the countries do not fulfill their debts, Mr. Sheridan will ask the Hague World Court to make this declaration.

▲Reuter, Salt Lake City, 18th. Republican Senator Smuder expressed his opinion on the war debt issue today, saying that if any country fails to clear its debts in accordance with the debt repayment agreement, the United States may conclude a reorganization law with each debtor country, but it should also be based on its ability to pay. It is an attitude of wanting Europe to repay its debts.

Debts Due Must Be Paid 61

▲Reuter, Washington, 17th. The State Department notified the French and Belgian ambassadors that the US government is not yet prepared to reply to their governments' requests to extend the debt repayment period and modify war debts. There is also news from New York that the United States will insist that Europe pay the debts due in December. The New York Tribune reported that President Hoover had discussed with his advisors and heard that if Europe wants to consider modifying the debt repayment conditions, it should first pay the debt due in November. According to the opinion of Hoover's friends, if Roosevelt does not agree to restore the Debt Repayment Committee during the meeting at the White House tomorrow, Hoover will abandon the proposal to restore the committee.

Reuter, London, 17th. The war debt issue still seems to be shrouded in haze in various markets. The London Stock Exchange and various commodities exchanges have limited transactions and prices are difficult to maintain. British government bonds continued to close slightly lower than yesterday. German government bonds also fell due to the political turmoil caused by Papen's resignation. The trend on Wall Street is uncertain.

Important News

Chiang Kai-shek Inspects Northern Hubei 68

Summons Frontline Generals

Instructs on Bandit Suppression Strategies

Hankou Correspondence: The communist bandits Xu Xiangqian and He Long joined forces two months ago and roamed through Suixian, Fancheng, and Guanghua in northern Hubei, splitting into three routes to infiltrate Shaanxi. One route was blocked and forced to return, fleeing to the border of Henan. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, in order to completely eradicate the bandit menace, specially dispatched eight divisions led by Hu Zongnan, Liu Maoen, Liu Chunlin, Xiao Zhichu, Fan Shisheng, Li Mo'an, Li Sizhuo, and Liu Kan (formerly General Fu Sheng) to encircle and suppress them. He also ordered the Shaanxi army to block key points, aiming to completely eliminate the remaining bandits within the current month. The bandits, facing a life-or-death situation, engaged in fierce battles with the National Army along the way. The Xu bandits are currently in the Kangjiaping and Renling Mountains, west of Zhaojia Street and east of Manchuan Pass. The First Division of the National Army under Hu Zongnan has advanced to the line of Sanshidian, Leiyin Temple, Qiliyanz, and Tianpeng Mountain. A part of the Eleventh Route Army has advanced to the line of Mahui River, Dagukou, and Dang Mountain. The 44th Division under Xiao Zhichu has advanced to the line of Zhangjiazhuang and Majiawan. The 51st Division under Fan Shisheng has advanced from the west to Tumen Town and Xiaxiangkou Town. The Shaanxi army is guarding the vicinity of Manchuan Pass with one brigade, and another brigade has advanced south from Shanyang to Shiyao, having established contact with other armies to encircle the bandits. The area has been experiencing cold rainy and snowy weather for days, and the officers and soldiers, barefoot and in thin clothing, are eagerly pursuing and suppressing the bandits, enduring hardships. The bandits are now trapped in the center of the encirclement with no way to escape but still rely on their large number of over ten thousand (some say Xu and He have a total of forty thousand) with complete weaponry to attempt a breakout to the west. In the coming days, there will be more bloody battles between the soldiers and bandits. The bandits fleeing to Henan are He Long's fake Seventh and Eighth Divisions. The fake Eighth Division has fled to Shuanghe Town in the northwest of Tongbai County, and the fake Seventh Division has fled to Haozhai in the southeast of Fangcheng County. Ma Hongkui dispatched Ma Yingcai's brigade to suppress them, defeating the bandits separately. In the battle of Haozhai, the fake Seventh Division Commander Tan Su and two fake regimental commanders, Sun Lingzhong and Shen Rong, were killed on the spot. Over three hundred bandits were killed and countless wounded. The remaining bandits have fled to the Shitouzhai at the junction of Nanyang and Fangcheng, where Ma's brigade is in hot pursuit. Judging from the current bandit situation, it is easier to eliminate He's bandits in southern Henan, while Xu's bandits are trying to penetrate deep into central Shaanxi to cross the Wei River and flee north. If they succeed, the communist disaster will spread to the northwest. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is determined to eradicate the bandits completely. In order to understand the military situation on the front lines, he departed from Hankou by his private plane at 10:00 AM on the 17th to inspect the area of Laohekou. Zhang Jianmeng, captain of the Sixth Aviation Squadron, piloted a plane in advance. It was reported that he had arrived there at noon and immediately summoned He Chengjun and other generals to instruct them on strategies. He is expected to return to Hankou by the original plane on the 18th or 19th and then go to Jiangxi for inspection at a later date. Zhang Xueliang, who came to Hankou to meet Chiang, will return to Beiping after Chiang returns to Hankou. Zhang has come to Hankou twice recently. The first time was on the 10th of this month, arriving from Pingnan by air and staying in Hankou for three days, meeting Chiang twice. On the 13th, he went to Hangzhou for sightseeing. The second time he came to Hankou to meet Chiang once. Zhang stays at the Central Bank when not busy and often amuses himself with little Gaoerfu. (November 17th)

Bandit Activities Flare Up Again in Rizhao 69

Qingdao Correspondence: The bandit leaders Yu Gongfang, An Fengduo, Zheng Guohong, and Zheng Tianjiu in Rizhao gathered crowds to wreak havoc on the 15th of last month, killing, setting fires, and looting civilian self-defense firearms, almost spreading throughout the county. Subsequently, Zhan Shutang, commander of the 81st Division stationed in Yishui, led his troops to suppress them, and the bandit forces were defeated and fled into the mountains. Commander Zhan pursued them repeatedly, killing over two hundred bandits. All the important bandit leaders fled. Commander Zhan, in addition to offering rewards for their capture, also left a battalion of soldiers to be responsible for rural pacification. Commander Zhan himself then quickly returned to Yishui with his troops to prevent further incidents. Unexpectedly, after Commander Zhan returned to defend, the remnants of the bandits revived. Recently, they joined forces with local bandits in the western mountains, relying on the mountains and forests to kidnap and demand ransoms. The kidnapped women are kept as wives and not allowed to be redeemed. A daughter of the Ma family in the Naxiang Quanzi area was kidnapped a few days ago. The Ma family prepared 1,500 yuan, intending to redeem their daughter, but the bandits kept 500 yuan and returned the remaining 1,000 yuan, saying it was a bride price for taking her as a wife. A daughter of the Qin family in Xinzhuang was also kidnapped by the bandits and her whereabouts are still unknown. The total number of women kidnapped from other villages is no less than several dozen. The bandits secretly sent their associates to incite unemployed people to join them, and many have joined. On the 10th of this month, the bandits held a meeting at the Nanshan Temple in Shanyuhe, attended by over two thousand people. After the meeting, they split into groups to kidnap and loot, looting Dashetou Village, Gao Village, Jin Village, Ma Village, Dapo Village, Xinliu Village, and Houtushan Village, and kidnapping over forty men and women. Wang Jiajue's family in Wangjia Village, a village about a mile away from Jiacang Town, was also quite wealthy and was recently kidnapped and ransomed for 10,000 yuan, which has not yet been redeemed. It is reported that the bandits are still being commanded by An Fengduo and Zheng Tianjiu. Currently, the people of Rizhao cannot sleep peacefully. Those with assets have already fled, and only middle and lower-class families remain, unable to leave and subject to the bandits' control. If the authorities do not quickly suppress them, they may become a major problem. (November 16th)

▲Major Theft Case at the Postal Bureau Solved: The case of a major theft at the local postal bureau at the end of last year, in which the iron box was broken open and a large amount of money was stolen, was reported to the county public security bureau, which ordered a strict investigation. The case remained unsolved for a long time and was repeatedly urged by the province. It has recently been learned that Yang Shijie, an inspector of the county public security bureau, arrested Tang Jinxiang, a habitual high-rise climber, based on information from an informant. According to his confession, he admitted that he stole 190 yuan in silver dollars, 280 yuan in banknotes, and 80 yuan in small notes in the postal bureau case last year, and divided it into five shares. Shen A'er, Tang Guisheng, Zhu Baoshan, and himself each received a share of 130 yuan, and another share was given to the person who climbed the wall. He also admitted that he stole one ten-yuan banknote, six five-yuan banknotes, fourteen one-yuan banknotes, forty-two yuan in silver dollars, six dimes in small notes, and sixteen dimes from the Texaco kerosene store on West Street on the evening of the 5th of last month, and divided it into four shares, with Zhu Baoshan receiving two shares. At the same time, he plotted to steal from Chengda Qianzhuang and Zhu Rizhang Cloth Store, but was discovered by his accomplices and fled. He also confessed that the cases of theft of clothing from the Jiang family and Peng family on the Cross Street outside the West Gate and the Qian Neixing leather clothing store outside the North Gate were all committed by them. It is reported that the public security bureau will transfer the case to the court for investigation as soon as the investigation is completed.

▲Director of the Finance Bureau Dies of Illness in Hangzhou: Xiao Zengrong, director of the local finance bureau, was old and ill. He went to Hangzhou for medical treatment. Yesterday, the bureau received a telegram informing them that Xiao had died of illness in Hangzhou. The provincial government ordered Feng Xiaobai, the chief of the bureau's section, to temporarily take over the director's duties, and a successor will be selected and sent to Songjiang soon.

Kunshan 72

▲Fraudulent Establishment of a Farm: Jiao from Beijie in the city falsely established a Limin Farm, advertising widely in Shanghai newspapers to recruit staff, each paying a registration fee of one yuan. Many unemployed people went to register and pay the fee. Bureau Chief Jie of the Public Security Bureau learned of this and immediately sent Inspector Zhang Bei and police to the bureau to interrogate Jiao. According to Jiao's confession, he admitted to the fraud. Bureau Chief Zhang considered the matter to be a fraudulent act and submitted a document to the county government for legal action.

▲Robbery of Rice Boats at Shian Bridge: Shian Bridge in Jiaqiao Township, is a remote area. On the morning of the 17th, a bandit boat suddenly moored there, with eleven armed bandits on board. At that time, a large group of farmers happened to be passing through the town by boat to sell rice. They were intercepted by the bandits. The farmers did not dare to resist, resulting in the robbery of thirteen rice boats, with a loss of more than three thousand yuan. After the robbery, they roared and left towards the Dianshan River.

Taicang 73

▲Wu Zigeng's Home Robbed Again: Wu Zigeng's home, a farmer in Nanxiang, Shuangfeng Town, was robbed once this spring. Unexpectedly, a dozen bandits speaking with Jiangbei and Shanghai accents robbed his home again in the middle of the night on the 16th. Four bandits wearing Luzon hats and masks. Neighbors rang gongs to call for help. The bandits immediately opened fire to intimidate them. Wu's wife was stopped by the bandits and forced to hand over the hidden money, robbing more than nine hundred yuan in cash. They left after half an hour. Afterwards, the incident was reported by the owner to the local public security branch, which forwarded it to the county government for investigation.

The Taiping Township part of the four-county boundary issue is the most important. Nan and Feng counties should first negotiate a solution and report it to this meeting, which will then convene another meeting. ㈡ Songjiang should still be invited to attend the next meeting.

▲Investigation of Construction Bureau Chief for Embezzlement: Yao Pengnian, the former director of the Construction Bureau, embezzled over 10,000 yuan and fled. Jiangyin 76

▲County Chamber of Commerce Demands Repayment of Loans: The County Chamber of Commerce had previously borrowed 5,000 yuan from various businesses for the security corps to go to Nantong, as decided by the county government conference. The loan has been overdue for two months. The debt has been repeatedly demanded but has not been repaid. In addition, 2,900 yuan is still owed for food expenses during the tenure of Xu Jiaxiu, the former fortress commander. The loan has been repaid with central bank checks but the checks are overdue for almost a year. The military and finance departments have been repeatedly telegraphed to order payment, but payment depends on the availability of funds allocated by the Ministry of Finance. Yesterday (16th), a meeting was held to demand repayment again and to send the approved situation to each borrower for verification.

▲Examination Confirms Murder of Husband: He Yunlin, from Baishali outside the East Gate, worked as a dyeing vat clerk at Tongfeng Cloth Factory outside the South Gate. He lived in Chenjia Village, Daihe. After drinking with friends at Xinxinyuan on the evening of the 11th, he went home and died suddenly overnight. When his brother, He Xulin, and others were preparing the body for burial the next day, they found wounds on Yunlin's body and suspected that his wife, Chen, had murdered him. They reported Chen and a suspect, Kou Shiyuan, to the Public Security Bureau, which forwarded it to the county on the 16th. After being summoned by Assessor Wang Chengzheng and testified by a group of witnesses, they were willing to sign a counter-charge agreement. At about 1:00 PM on the 17th, Assessor Wang and Examiner Cao, along with the deceased's wife, Chen, and others, went to Yujia Village in Baishali and exhumed the coffin. Upon opening the coffin, an examination revealed a sharp-edged wound on the right back of the head, measuring seven inches long, two inches deep, and three inches wide. Two silver hairpins were inserted into the mouth and anus for examination, as required by law. Black matter was found that could not be washed away with soapberry water. The examiner reported that the death was due to a poisonous blade wound to the brain. After the examination, the body was collected by the deceased's mother, He Xu. Returned to the county government at about 6:00 PM.

Wuxi 77

▲Reorganization of Salt Affairs Tax Police District: Zhang Zhongli, director of the Tax Police Bureau of the Songjiang Salt Affairs Audit Office of the Ministry of Finance, recently ordered Chen Junxia, director of the Eighth District stationed in Wuxi, to be transferred to the bureau as a counselor. The district headquarters will be abolished and reorganized into a second-class sub-district headquarters, which will be under the jurisdiction of the Sixth District and named the First Sub-District of the Sixth District. Another person, Chen Wei, was appointed to fill the vacancy of sub-district director. The former first, third, fourth, and fifth teams under the former Eighth District were reorganized into the sixth, seventh, eighth, and ninth teams of the Sixth District, all under the command of Chen Wei, who also served as the captain of the sixth team. The former Eighth District's second team leader, Tang Shaoxian, and deputy team leader, Huang Yuanji, stationed in Dangkou were ordered to be transferred to Suzhou Zhujing for reorganization. After receiving the order, Chen Wei came to Wuxi to take office. He has now reported to the district director of the Sixth District for transfer to Director Zhang for verification and approval. The seal will be put into use immediately. The day before yesterday, Chen again ordered Sun Wenxiang, the captain of the seventh team, to be transferred to Dangkou and yesterday accompanied the district headquarters officials to inspect the area under their jurisdiction in order to consolidate it.

▲Organization of the National Products Promotion Preparatory Committee: The local County Chamber of Commerce had previously received a telegram from the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce requesting the joint organization of a National Products Promotion Committee. The Chamber submitted it to the eighth executive supervisory meeting, which resolved to organize a preparatory committee and appointed Wu Shimei, Hua Shaochun, Cheng Jingtang, Jiang Jinghai, Jiang Zhongliang, Qian Jingsheng, Qian Furen, Cai Yong, and Chen Zhanru as members of the preparatory committee. Hua Shaochun convened a meeting yesterday, and the County Chamber of Commerce sent letters to Wu Shimei and others for verification and implementation.

▲Zhou Limen Escapes from Bandit Lair: Zhou Haoen, the owner of Renhe Smoke Shop in Luoshe, Sixteenth District, has accumulated considerable savings in recent years. Last month, his wife, Tang, took his beloved son, Limen (fifteen years old), back to his original home in Yangzhong. Unexpectedly, they were robbed and Limen was kidnapped. Within a few days, the bandits sent a letter demanding a ransom of 50,000 yuan. If the deadline was exceeded, they would tear up the ticket. Zhou was extremely anxious because he had no money to raise. However, Limen suddenly returned safely to his home in Luoshe the day before yesterday. The family was overjoyed at the reunion, and Tang's illness suddenly disappeared after the surprise. Upon questioning, it was learned that Limen had been closely guarded on the bandit ship after being kidnapped, traveling to the countryside of Jiangyin. Until the day before yesterday, when the bandits went ashore to rob again, Limen took the opportunity to go ashore and escaped home.

[Changzhou]

▲Anti-Japanese Association's Measures for Dealing with Enemy Goods: The Wuyi Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association convened a representatives' meeting on the morning of the 17th to discuss measures for dealing with enemy goods. It was decided that: ㈠ All businesses unsealing enemy goods should immediately establish public sales departments. ㈡ For unscrupulous merchants who delay paying fines, measures such as sealing the store, confiscating the goods, detaining people, and standing on wooden boards will be implemented. ㈢ Cotton and nylon cloth factories that sell enemy goods under a different brand will be severely investigated by the next executive committee. Finally, it was resolved to comply with the provincial regulations on the organization of anti-Japanese national salvation associations and to appoint two members from the County Party Department, one from the County Chamber of Commerce, one from the County Farmers' Association, one from the County Education Association, one from the Student Union, one from the Guild, and one from free professions and cultural organizations as executive members of the Anti-Japanese Association.

▲Finance Bureau Sends Personnel to Rural Areas to Expedite Tax Collection: The Jiangdu County Finance Bureau, because repeated announcements to expedite the completion of tax payments this year have yielded few results, and the collection of arrears over the years has also been unsuccessful, in addition to sending personnel to sit at the counter to supervise the collection, yesterday specially dispatched several personnel carrying the bureau's printed exhortations to the public to quickly pay this year's land tax to various townships for propaganda.

▲Construction Department Plans to Renovate Stonework Project with Funds: Construction Department Director Dong Xiujia believes that the breach in the Shangyou military building is the most dangerous and should be renovated with stonework to achieve a permanent solution. ▲Discovery of a Giant Python with Two Horns on its Head: A giant python with two horns on its head, about two zhang long and as thick as a bowl, with a black body and white markings, was discovered in Xiaocun, west of Chemalake Town River. It was killed by local villagers with farming tools. A crowd gathered to watch, surprised by this rare sight.

A handgun was found on Lu, and multiple letters plotting to kidnap Li Tingbin's son for ransom were found in his trunk. Pinghu 81

▲National Salvation Corps Warns Unscrupulous Merchants: Dafeng and Guanghua Sock Factories in the city secretly imported Japanese yarn and were repeatedly caught but have not been punished. A few days ago, Guanghua again imported two hundred bundles of Japanese yarn and was still seized. Gao Dengfu and two other members of the Anti-Japanese Association Standing Committee considered it domestic goods and allowed them to be returned. However, Yang, an executive member of the association, insisted that it was definitely Japanese goods. The Executive Committee, led by Xia Yuchang, carefully unpacked and counted each bundle when returning them and discovered the Toyota Yarn Company trademarks of Japanese merchants that had not been completely torn off. It was then retained and referred to the County Party Department for further action. Yesterday, on the Hanshui Bridge in the bustling city, a large advertisement of the National Salvation and Elimination of Traitors Corps was suddenly seen, severely criticizing both parties involved, denouncing Li Zhi, the owner of Dafeng, as a unscrupulous merchant and denouncing Gao Dengfu and Lu Gongliang of the Anti-Japanese Association as corrupt members. The advertisement has been posted for two days and has not dared to be removed to this day.

Taixian 84

▲County Government Mediates Sanli Han Dispute: Sanli Han in the west of Haian Town in the county collapsed due to a flood, becoming a river channel that ships could pass through directly. As a result, cargo ships passing through the Han also passed without stopping. The operators of the guozai (ferry) business in the area, who benefited from the passage of the transport ships, advocated opening the Han, while the porters and coolies of Wuli, whose livelihood depended on it, strongly opposed it. The dispute between the two sides intensified, leading to the coolies gathering over a hundred people to demand a strike, and the guozai business also put up signs saying 放载. Hearing this, the county government sent personnel to the area to convene a meeting of various agencies, groups, and representatives from both sides to discuss the opening and closing of the Han in order to resolve the dispute. It is believed that this dispute will not be difficult to resolve.

Hefei 85

▲Directors of Three-County Beneficial Bureaus Have Been Appointed: Wang Daren, the Chief County Magistrate of Hefei who also serves as the Special Commissioner for the seven counties in western Anhui, is sparing no effort in handling the aftermath in Liuan, Huoshan, and Huoqiu. In addition to ordering the County Magistrate of Huoqiu to quickly recover 10,000 yuan misappropriated from last year's flood relief funds in order to be used for relief, he has also established Beneficial Bureaus in Liuan, Huoshan, and Huoqiu with 5,000 yuan recently allocated by the Finance Department for the benefit of disaster victims in the aftermath of the disaster. Kong Shuzeng and Liu Jisanzhou have been appointed as the directors of the Huoqiu Beneficial Bureau, Wang Dufeng has been appointed as the director of the Liuan City Beneficial Bureau, Wu Xian'gen has been appointed as the director of the Huoshan City Beneficial Bureau, and Zuo Chuseng has been appointed as the director of the Zhufu An Beneficial Branch Bureau in Huojing. Liao Huanong has been appointed as a member of the planning committee for the opening of the Beneficial Bureaus in the three counties and will be leaving in the coming days.

▲Yang's Brigade Suppresses Zhang and Xie's Bandit Gangs: The Zhang Dabizi and Xie Wudai bandit gangs, which have been disrupting the counties of He, Liu, Shu, and Shou, recently fled to Fanghu Mountain Xie Ancestral Hall. They were surrounded and suppressed by Yang's Brigade of the 55th Division, and dozens of bandits were killed. Xie Wudai was killed in battle, and Zhang Dabizi was injured and led the remaining bandits to break through the encirclement and flee. Yang's Brigade captured Zhou Jipu and Ge Mingyou and handed them over to the city. After being interrogated by the military law department, they were sentenced to death and shot at Ducaidatang on the 13th. In addition, Ruan Zhaochang, commander of the 55th Division, who accompanied Chen Tiaoyuan to Hankou to meet Chairman Chiang, had returned to Hefei for defense on the 13th.

Letter of Reply

Letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Government 86

To the Editor:

The Jiangsu Province Regulations for Pawnshop Operations were amended and promulgated by the Provincial Government Committee at its 372nd meeting on February 10, 20th year of the Republic (1931). Currently, industrial and commercial matters are handled by the Department of Industry, and all references to the Department of Construction in the original regulations have been changed to the Department of Industry. There have been no other changes to the articles. It is inaccurate to say that new regulations have recently been drafted. This is hereby communicated for your information and publication in the letter column to clarify the facts. Secretariat of the Jiangsu Provincial Government.

Educational News

Important News 87

Jiangsu Province Prohibits Students from Suspending Classes and Soliciting Donations 88

Zhenjiang, 18th: The Jiangsu Provincial Government held its 544th meeting on the 18th, chaired by Gu Zhutong, and resolved that: ㈠ All county military and political officers are ordered to issue notices prohibiting students from suspending classes, leaving school, forming teams, and soliciting donations. If such incidents occur, they should be stopped by force and forcibly dispersed. In addition, no organization may solicit donations freely without the approval of the government.

Representatives of Primary and Secondary Schools in Beiping Arrive in Nanjing to Petition 89

Nanjing, 18th: Li Jinghan, Feng Liuxi, and Yao Shouqi, representatives of the Joint Association of Primary and Secondary Schools in Beiping, arrived in Nanjing on the 18th. They will petition the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Education within the next few days to urge the issuance of subsidized funds. According to a reporter, the expenses of primary and secondary schools in Beiping were initially provided by the Chongguan customs revenue. Since the abolition of the Chongguan customs revenue in the 18th year of the Republic (1929), they have relied on a monthly subsidy of 50,000 yuan from the central government to barely maintain. In recent months, the central government has not issued the subsidies as scheduled, and Beiping's finances are extremely difficult, resulting in teachers' salaries being in arrears for several months. The teachers are unable to make a living, so they have specially sent representatives to Nanjing to urge the issuance of subsidized funds, hoping that the central government will consider the tens of thousands of students in primary and secondary schools in Beiping and immediately allocate funds to maintain them.

Beiping, 18th: Li Zheng went to Beijing to discuss with various parties about the Ministry of Education's change to the organization of the Normal University. The Ministry of Education Cracks Down on Private Schools in Beijing 91

Nanjing, 18th: The Ministry of Education has sent personnel to thoroughly investigate education in Beijing. Private schools with a profit motive will be severely cracked down on.

Promulgation of Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum Standards by the Ministry of Education (2) 92

One. Kindergarten Curriculum Standards

First, Overall Goals of Kindergarten Education

(1) To enhance the physical and mental health of young children.

(2) To strive for the joy and happiness that young children should have.

(3) To cultivate basic good habits in life (including habits in all aspects such as physical behavior).

(4) To assist families in raising young children and to seek improvement in family education.

Second, Curriculum Scope

(1) Music

I. Goals: A. To satisfy the desire to sing. B. To inspire and enhance the ability to appreciate music (including both vocal and instrumental). C. To develop vocal abilities and the sense of rhythm, and to train rhythmic movements. D. To develop feelings of love and cooperation. E. To arouse interest in things (such as cats, dogs, farming, washing clothes, etc.).

II. Content Outline: A. Listening, singing, performing, and appreciating various lyrics (a) about family life (b) about commemorations and celebrations (c) about seasons and festivals (d) about natural phenomena (e) about common flora and fauna (f) about daily work (g) about patriotism (h) about social interaction (i) for performance purposes. B. Listening and performing rhythmically. C. Appreciating and performing common music (small gongs, small drums, wooden fish, etc. can all be used) (e.g., sitting, standing, and walking according to the sound). D. Appreciating and imitating natural sounds (such as bird songs and cat meows).

III. Minimum Requirements: A. Clear singing and generally accurate rhythm. B. Ability to distinguish and respond to simple rhythms (fast, slow, high, low, etc.). C. Understanding the meaning of four or more lyrics and being able to perform them. D. Ability to sing two simple lyrics solo.

(2) Stories and Nursery Rhymes

I. Goals: A. To arouse interest in literature. B. To develop imagination. C. To inspire thought. D. To practice speaking and enhance the ability to express oneself. E. To develop the ability to create stories and cultivate emotions such as joy, nobility, and love.

II. Content Outline: A. Appreciating and practicing various stories (e.g., oral narration, performance, creation, etc.) (a) fairy tales (b) nature stories (c) historical stories (d) life stories (e) folk tales (f) jokes (g) fables. B. Reading various story picture cards. C. Appreciating, chanting, and performing various interesting but not vulgar children's songs and riddles.

III. Minimum Requirements: A. Ability to narrate four of the simplest stories with clear meaning. B. Ability to create one of the simplest stories with obvious content. C. Ability to make simple and clear responses.

(3) Games

I. Goals: A. To cater to the natural inclination to enjoy games and provide appropriate game activities. B. To develop the coordinated function of muscles and train the sensitive response of senses and limbs. C. To train social skills such as mutual assistance and cooperation.

II. Content Outline: Practice various games: A. Counting games (e.g., throwing a ball can also practice counting). B. Story performance and singing expression games. C. Rhythmic (e.g., games that make birds fly and animals walk according to the sound) and non-dancing games. D. Sensory games (games that practice touch, hearing, and sight, such as touching in the dark and finding people by listening). E. Games using simple equipment (such as swings and slides). F. Imitation games (imitating actions such as soldiers drilling and cats catching mice). G. Various good games inherent in various regions of our country.

III. Minimum Requirements: A. Ability to participate in the assembly, lining up, and circling of children and feel coordinated. B. Ability to use three or more of the play equipment provided in the kindergarten. C. Knowing the simple rules of the game.

(4) Society and Nature

I. Goals: A. To guide the observation and appreciation of the natural environment and people's activities. B. To enhance the initial experience of utilizing nature to satisfy life and organize groups. C. To guide the understanding of the relationship between "man, society, and nature." D. To develop good habits such as caring for natural objects and being hygienic and gregarious.

II. Content Outline: A. Observing and studying daily necessities such as food, clothing, shelter, and transportation, hygiene methods, and social organizations such as families, neighborhoods, shops, post offices, fire-fighting organizations, parks, and transportation agencies, and touring local scenic spots and historical sites. B. Practicing daily etiquette. C. Studying and holding commemorative days and festivals (such as New Year's Day, National Day, the anniversary of the death and birth of the Premier, May Ninth, May Thirtieth, Children's Day, and other seasonal festivals). D. Understanding the parts of the body and simple hygiene rules (such as not eating sweets from street vendors, not eating miscellaneous foods, washing hands before meals, washing face after meals, not urinating or spitting anywhere, not picking the ears or rubbing the eyes with hands, going to bed early and getting up early, and loving cleanliness). E. Checking health and cleanliness. F. Recognizing the Party flag, the national flag, the Premier's portrait, etc. G. Recognizing and studying common birds, beasts, insects, fish, flowers, trees, and natural phenomena such as the sun, moon, rain, snow, cloudy and sunny weather, wind, and clouds. H. Daily recording of the month, week, day, and daily weather conditions such as sunny, cloudy, rainy, and snowy. I. Observing, collecting, and raising or cultivating plants and animals in the vicinity or in the kindergarten. J. Practicing gatherings (mainly to cultivate attitudes and spirits of fairness, love, peace).

III. Minimum Requirements: (A) To recognize the main items of clothing, food, shelter, and transportation used in one's daily life. (B) To know a little about the functions of families, neighborhoods, shops, factories, farms, and local public institutions. (C) To know the functions of the limbs and five senses. (D) To recognize domestic fowl and livestock and five or more plants, as well as the functions of the sun, wind, and rain. (E) To recognize the Premier's portrait and the Party flag and national flag. (F) To have considerable politeness towards teachers and parents. (G) To have a habit of cleanliness.

(5) Work

I. Goals: (A) To satisfy the natural need for work. (B) To cultivate operational habits, enhance work skills, and exercise sensory abilities; to develop basic gross motor skills as the foundation for the development of fine motor skills in the future; to provide opportunities for various physical and mental movements to be performed often. (C) To train group activity, for example, a spirit of self-confidence, self-respect, perseverance, concentration, diligence, mutual assistance, and enthusiastic service; the ability to act autonomously; the spirit of leadership talent and obedience to the leader; the ability to criticize and the measure to accept criticism; the habit of not wasting time and materials; the habit of obeying orders; loving public utensils. (D) To develop intelligence, for example, to train thought; to cultivate the ability to express, create, and construct; to develop the ability to appreciate.

II. Content Outline: Children should do any work within the following scope according to their preferences: (A) Sandbox Installation: Arranging and stacking various toy items in a sandbox or sand table to observe and study many three-dimensional things that have been observed and studied, such as villages, cities, mountain scenes, garden scenes, rivers, animal farms, botanical gardens, or other models, etc. (B) Gift Installation: Using blocks of various sizes to build houses and other buildings, etc. (C) Drawing: Free monochrome or color drawing. Various ready-made pictures and objects can be used for color drawing so that children can set colors themselves or use their own drawings and objects to apply colors. (D) Paper Crafts: Using scissors to cut various shapes or folding various objects with paper (such as tables, chairs, etc.), or gluing the cut, folded, or torn shapes on paper with paste, or using paper strips to form various patterns. (E) Clay and Pulp Crafts: Using clay or paper pulp to make models, such as chickens, dogs, peaches, plums, cups, plates, cakes, biscuits, boats, cars, etc., and studying the properties of clay. (F) Sewing: The motivation for sewing usually comes from playing with dolls, such as decorating dollhouses or making small clothes, small quilts, and small curtains for dolls. This work should be done by older children. Younger children can use cardboard to prick holes to make apples, carrots, or cats and hounds, and let them weave with colored threads. (G) Carpentry: Using simple woodworking tools such as awls and saws, and being able to plan and make several simple toy models (such as beds, tables, chairs, swing sets, etc.), and knowing the methods and order of doing them (for example, knowing that the four legs of a table should be the same length, the ratio of the tabletop to the legs should be appropriate, and the four legs should be nailed under the tabletop, etc.). (H) Weaving: Being able to use the thickest shuttle to weave thread and ribbon, etc. (I) Gardening: Planting vegetables, planting beans, planting ordinary flowers, etc. (J) Other: Using various natural objects and waste materials to make toys and decorations, etc. (Note) It is best to have all of the above types of work, but they can be selected according to the situation of the environment.

III. Minimum Requirements: (A) Ability to do simple work alone without seeking assistance from others. (B) Ability to cherish tools and materials. (C) Ability to organize tools, materials, and works and to place tools, materials, and works in their places. (D) Ability to keep the ground clean. (E) Ability to not dirty the body and clothes. (F) Ability to use pencils or crayons. (G) Ability to use scissors. (H) Ability to choose colors. (I) Ability to arrange graphics. (J) Ability to grow one or two kinds of vegetables or flowers. (To be continued)

The Municipal School Implements Hygiene Work 98

▲ It will start next Monday

Li Ting'an, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, and Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, discussed and decided on a method of proceeding, given the importance of school hygiene. Sun Jiaqi, Director of the School Hygiene Section of the Health Bureau, will begin work next Monday. A Central News Agency reporter interviewed Li Ting'an, Director of the Health Bureau, yesterday to inquire about the methods of carrying out school hygiene. According to Li, school hygiene is extremely important, and the learning ability of students will be greatly affected if it is not properly promoted. Although the school hygiene work in this city has been gradually expanded to 20 schools four years ago, it is still far from the number of schools in this city. This is due to funding issues that are still being planned and promoted. However, since the January 28th Incident, the bureau's funding has been tight, and many students have suspended classes, so the work has been temporarily suspended. The Education Bureau and schools in this city attach great importance to this cause, so the results of cooperation over the years have been quite good. This year, the Education Bureau has also stipulated that it is the annual Health Education Center, so after taking office, I believe that this cause can no longer be delayed and I am determined to resume and promote it. I have now discussed it with Director Pan of the Education Bureau and received his approval. It will be implemented in the near future, and it is planned to implement school hygiene in the municipal schools in the Nanshi, Zhabei, and Gaoqiao districts as the first phase, totaling 67 schools with approximately 20,000 students. The promotion method is that the school authorities are responsible for the central responsibility, and the Health Bureau will send specially trained personnel to plan and guide them to facilitate implementation. The technical aspects will also be handled by personnel sent by the Health Bureau. The work that should be done includes physical examinations, early treatment, and correction of physical defects, such as instilling hygiene knowledge and training to develop good hygiene habits, such as cleaning up the school environment to avoid harming the health of students, such as improving nutrition to avoid causing anemia or lung disease, such as using various methods to develop health levels and enhance learning ability. Sun Jiaqi, Director of the School Hygiene Section of this bureau, has been sent to Nanjing last week to investigate and is expected to return to Shanghai around Saturday of this week, and will start work next Monday. Li also said that it is rumored that the funding for this work is borne by the American oil king, etc. This is a rumor and is wrong. This bureau has not received any subsidies from the oil king. Only when the school hygiene and rural hygiene work in the Gaoqiao district were established in this city in the 18th year of the Republic of China, the International Health Society subsidized all the start-up costs and the first year's recurring expenses and half of the second year's recurring expenses. This was discussed and obtained by the former Director Hu. As for the nature of the International Health Society, it can also be said for you by the way that the society is allocated a large fund by the oil king to subsidize medical and health undertakings in various countries. If an application is made to the society for a subsidy of funds, it can be approved for a considerable subsidy after the society considers it appropriate. This situation is not limited to any country. Many medical or health undertakings in various countries have received their assistance. The restoration of school hygiene this time is all funded by the municipal government and is the responsibility of the Education and Health Bureaus, and there is no subsidy from the society.
