West Lake Art School Volleyball Team Suffers Another Defeat to Daxia Yesterday 111

The Hangzhou Art School volleyball team has been fighting hard in consecutive battles. Yesterday, the team suffered another defeat to Daxia. In this game, Daxia's Wei Dingyi and Chen Baoqiu's spikes were like iron hammers, while Art School's Guan Qinghua and Wu Yisun's slices were like steel knives. Both sides were evenly matched. Daxia won the first set, boosting their momentum. Unexpectedly, Art School responded with color, working hard to counterattack and winning back the second set, tying the score at 1-1. At this time, the battle became tense, with fierce exchanges and a struggle for survival. Sydney, 17th - The entire American lawn tennis team has invaded Australia to participate in the New South Wales competition. Fanhns and Ellison have reached the semi-finals. In the quarter-finals, Ellison defeated Australian general Crawford with a score of 7-5, 4-6, 6-2, 4-6, 6-3. Fanhns defeated Fanling with a score of 8-6, 6-4, 3-6, 6-0. The final will be held on Saturday (19th). The first game between the two teams is scheduled for November 24, 25, and 26 in Brisbane. The second game will be in Perth on December 4, 6, and 7. The third game will be in Adelaide on January 5, 6, and 7 next year. The fourth game will be in Sydney on January 12, 13, and 14. The fifth game will be in Melbourne on February 2, 3, and 4. The American team will leave Australia on February 10 or 11 and go to New Zealand, then travel to Japan for several performances before returning to the United States.

Therefore, although the market was active, the price was flat and soft. High-quality rice was still firmly standing. Tongjin was taken away by the Beiyang group. 750 bags of Huji red rice were priced at 8 yuan, 1 jiao to 7 yuan, 8 or 9 jiao, and 80 bags of Jiyuan rice were priced at 10 yuan, 4 jiao, 5 fen. The Fuzhou group took away 65 bags of Jiangxi Jiwan rice priced at 8 yuan, 6 jiao, 1,500 bags of Huji oil rice priced at 8 yuan, 9 jiao to 8 yuan, 8 jiao, 5 fen, and 50 bags of Jijing rice priced at 8 yuan, 3 jiao. 285 bags of Yun Jing rice were priced at 7 yuan, 1 jiao.

Consistent Decline in the Post-Market of Marked Flour 126

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month showed a trend of near stability and far decline. The international wheat price fell by about 3, 4, or 5 jiao. People inside and outside the industry were naturally unstable. The current month tended to be stable due to the relationship of spot goods. The poor situation of the distant months due to the slight selling of Fufeng and the continued surplus of the international wheat market can be seen from this. Therefore, each distant month fell by about 1 point. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the near and distant months were uniformly soft. It was rumored that Fufeng had imported foreign wheat and that the futures for the current month could be settled with a surplus (it was also rumored that the price of Australian wheat was loose to 3 taels, 4 qian, 5 fen). Therefore, the current month was gradually sold out, and the general idea of squeezing shorts was too much, resulting in great weakness. The market price fell step by step. The distant months, such as January and February, once entered the 7 qian gate, and after observing, followed the 4 qian, 5 fen foreign wheat again. If there were to be transactions, the market would be afraid of further changes. As a result, the current month fell sharply by 2 fen, December fell by 4 fen, January fell by 2 fen, 7 li, 5 hao, February fell by 2 fen, 5 hao, and March and April fell by 1 fen, 7 li, 5 hao.

Uniform Trend of Decline in Futures Wheat 127

After the opening of futures wheat yesterday morning and afternoon, each month generally showed a flat and tired trend. The quotation for foreign wheat fell again by a huge 3, 4, or 5 jiao. The surplus of international wheat production had not yet been resolved, and the road to gradual loosening was nothing more than an attempt to dump it in China. This situation was a hidden danger for the future. Therefore, although transactions in each month were not smooth, people's hearts had largely loosened. Fortunately, there were few real chips in the market, otherwise it would be unbearable to imagine. As a result, the current month fell by 2 fen compared to the previous day, January fell by 1 fen, and there was no rise or fall in February.

Chicago Wheat Bulls Take Profits 128

A report from Sin Fung Foreign Firm states that Chicago wheat fell by 1.5 to 1.875 points for each period on Friday due to bull profit-taking. On the 16th, a total of 20 million bushels were traded. The market prices on the 17th are listed below:

New Chaoqing Sugar Already Opened in the Sugar Market 129

│Ordinary Goods Priced at 9 Taels 6 Qian│

Yesterday, the sugar market saw a slight stabilization with the continued upward trend of the marked gold. The guild's pricing for 24 coarse sand white was 14 taels, 9 qian, 2 fen, 5 li for high-quality goods and 14 taels, 8 qian, 2 fen, 5 li for ordinary goods. 20 medium sand white was 14 taels, 3 qian, and 18 medium sand white was 14 taels. Only sporadic transactions occurred. No. 10 Dutch red was划划划 out by Changxing, a famous firm, at 11 taels 6 qian. Shaobang Tong Anhao opened a batch of New Chaoqing, which was ordinary in color and body, priced at only 9 taels 6 qian, and the receivers were not enthusiastic. Other goods were dull due to the weak market and lacked transactions.

The Market Sentiment for Nanbei Goods, Quanzhou Longans, and Bubbled Longans is Downward 130

The sales of Quanzhou large-bubbled longans have been sluggish recently, and very few of the branded goods have been opened, because the firms still have a lot of stock on hand and dare not be greedy for inventory. However, the firms are still watching because the cost of the goods is still a concern for the owners and they are unwilling to discount them. It is heard that the Funan and Huaping have imported in succession by sea from Quanzhou, and it is found that there are more than 2,000 boxes of bubbled longans being transported, so the market situation is even more tired. The goods that were at the top tier in the previous market were extremely strong, but now there is a gradual accumulation and the sales are also reduced. The market sentiment is downward.

Silk, Tea, Factory, and Warp Doors Have Smooth Sales 131

│Yesterday, 65 pieces of Yellow and White Factory Warps were Shipped to Hangzhou│

The silk weaving factories in Hangzhou are now weaving winter silk, and the consumption of factory warps is increasing day by day. The silk factories, in view of the tired trend in the market price of factory warps, have telegraphed Shanghai to take the opportunity to purchase them, so the current goods have been transacted daily and the silk warps transported to Hangzhou are not deserted. Yesterday, a certain transportation company also undertook the installation of 65 pieces of yellow and white factory warps purchased by various silk factories in Shanghai to Hangzhou.

There is Still No Turnaround in Silk Sales in Europe and America 132

Yesterday, there was still no turnaround in the silk market of foreign firms in this port. The raw silk factories in the overseas market were still lazy to enter the market, and the silk prices became more tired. The telegrams from Shanghai did not see any turnaround, so the market was depressed.

The Inventory of African Green Tea is Thin and Low 133

According to informed sources, the inventories of north and south Africa, which are major sellers of Zhenmei green tea of ​​gongse in my country, have recently been depleted. However, due to the poor harvest of various agricultural products such as rice and wheat in the road this year, the economy has declined, and the purchasing power has been reduced. British and French merchants who are currently operating on the road have the momentum to take advantage of the time to handle the waxing Zhenmei, but because the tea prices in Shanghai have fallen too quickly recently, they are deeply afraid of buying expensively, and they mostly hold a wait-and-see attitude. If the market stabilizes, the sales of Zhenmei in the future will have a major development.

The Prices of Piece Goods and Overcoat Naps are Inconsistent 134

Recently, the sales of overcoat naps have developed day by day, and the sales of men's and women's colored Chinese and Western suits have continued. However, the selling prices are inconsistent, depending on how large the inventory is and how strong the demand is. Most of the Western-style overcoat naps are sold at about 10 taels, and the market is very strong. The sales of women's overcoat naps with fresh patterns are also smooth. The overcoat naps of Chinese-style clothing on the main road have fallen by half, half of which is due to the influence of riding breeches overcoats and half due to the Great Reduction in business due to the war in the Guan Dong north port, and the prices of goods have been falling step by step.

Coal and Stove Coal Transactions are Booming 135

The weather has turned cold in recent days, and stoves are being launched on the market, so the coal market is also heating up for stove transactions. Yesterday, the city mostly opened with white coal, with a total of about 1,800 tons. Hongqi coal was the strongest, and the asking price was also good, and the price of each ton rose by 2 qian and a half. The market for Shanxi coal was also good, and the under-the-counter price rose by 5 fen. The number of transactions for smoke coal and domestic coal did not rise, and the most transactions for Fushun coal of Japanese coal, with a price of 10 taels, 5 qian per ton.

Local News

The Second Batch of Volunteer Army Aid Team Members Departed Last Night 155

▲To Bengbu to Join the Second Detachment, Heading Directly to the Battlefield. The second batch of the Northeast Volunteer Army Aid Team has completed all procedures and departed last night at 11:00 PM on the Shanghai-Nanjing overnight express train. They will first go to Bengbu to join with their Second Detachment, and then head directly from Bengbu to the battlefield to serve the anti-Japanese volunteer army. The location will be determined after the team leader, Fei Jian, goes to Peiping to meet with various anti-Japanese generals. The team also issued a declaration yesterday, stating:

▲List of Names of the Second Batch Departing Members: The list of members departing in the second batch is as follows: Huang Zhong, Wang Mengying, Huangfu Jun, Ji Huobin, Duan Jiamo, Xu Shida, Ye Keze, Liu Junpeng, Lu Dongshan, Chen Zhaohai, Wei Faliang, and 80 members of the Second Detachment in Bengbu, totaling 92 people. They are led by the team leader and Chen Ruchen of the Second Detachment, carrying over 30 large pieces of various supplies, departing from Shanghai at 11:00 PM last night.

▲All Sectors Enthusiastically Donate: Yesterday, colleagues from the Yong'an First Cotton Mill in this city donated 20 silver dollars and 40 bolts of flannel to the team, along with over a hundred yards of slightly damaged flannel and an accompanying letter. Furthermore, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association from all sectors of Hangzhou specially sent 135 pieces of confiscated Japanese surgical medical equipment yesterday, dispatching Executive Committee member Zhang Wanli to bring them to Shanghai and hand them over to the team. Other donors are as follows: Zhou Zige donated 2 silver dollars, Chengji Gong Rice Shop donated 1 silver dollar, Yangsentai donated 2 silver dollars, Ruihecheng, Tianfeng, Lao Yonghe, Chun Hexiang, Zhentai, Yuankang, Qun Yushanfang, Hualun, Zhaotai, Dachang, Wansheng, Jusheng, Xintianxiang, Xiesui, Fengtai, Yixingchang, Puli, each donating 1 silver dollar. He Hongtai, Erlingxuan, Zhuang Shunxiang, Yuanda, Hengde, Wang Renmao, Taifeng, Kecheng, Xinkangxiang, Wang Xintai, Tianchangxiang, Yuxingxiang, Xiudetang, Hongmaochang, Qingchangxiang, Sanyi, Yufengheng, Li Chuji, each donating 5 jiao.

▲The Team Issued a Declaration: Since the September 18th Incident, the court and the public have been stirred, the whole country is seething, the black current is wailing, and the green mountains have changed color. Looking remotely at the broken rivers and mountains of the Northeast, and the tragic and humiliating scene of the 30 million people, those with blood and vigor should not be muddleheaded, and those with national hatred and a sense of responsibility should not abandon their duty. Therefore, hundreds of thousands of Northeast Volunteer Army soldiers have risen up one after another, able to maintain their position against the powerful enemy for over a year with the spirit of courage and perseverance. Enduring hardship and difficulty, falling forward and following each other, only due to the lack of firearms and economic constraints, our respectable and lovable Northeast vanguard cannot fight in peace. The colleagues and others, seeing this, have organized the Northeast Volunteer Army Aid Team, not shirking any difficulties or pain, to fulfill the duty of every citizen and do our national duty. In the past few months, we have received enthusiastic assistance from all sectors and enthusiastic participation from comrades. The first batch went through customs on the day before last month to carry out aid work, and the second batch will also depart tonight (the 18th), all proficient in medicine and skilled in first aid, led by the team leader Fei Jian to Bengbu to gather at the Tongren Hospital. The third batch is being actively prepared and will rush north as soon as the organization is ready. The colleagues and others have limited talent and ability, and are sincerely afraid that the effect will not be great. We hope that our countrymen will remember this critical moment of survival, the wise will give their wisdom, and the brave will exert their strength, to encourage the courage of the volunteer army to engage in long-term confrontation, and to share the hardships with the volunteer army, providing first aid for wounds. Furthermore, the weather has been severely cold recently, and the volunteer army is still enduring hatred and hunger, thrusting straight forward in the icy and snowy fields. With broken bones and torn flesh, how can anyone not be moved? We sincerely hope that compatriots from all walks of life will rise up to assist, donating quilts and cotton clothing, providing a continuous supply of medicines and medical supplies, and especially generously donating money and enthusiastically transporting it, so that the soldiers in front can fight with peace of mind. We also hope that famous figures in the country will provide guidance so that the colleagues and others have a clear direction. This is our sincere hope.

Chinese Business Tram Workers Strike Yesterday Morning 156

▲Security Team and Workers

▲Both Sides Injured

▲Mayor Wu's Opinion

Yesterday, a labor dispute and bombing incident occurred at the Chinese Business Electric Company. The details of the incident and Mayor Wu's statement are described below.

▲Details of the Incident: Yesterday morning, a dispute arose at the Chinese Business Electric Company due to the loss of the tram car key. The factory and the workers immediately had a disagreement. The police station of the Second District Public Security Bureau, upon receiving the report, dispatched officers to investigate in order to maintain traffic. While investigating, the workers suddenly surrounded the office and demanded an immediate response to their demands for a pay raise from the general manager. The situation was extremely dangerous. The Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, immediately dispatched a police squadron to suppress the situation, but the workers were too numerous to be suppressed. The Security Department also dispatched the Tenth Squad of the Third Company of the First Regiment to assist at the scene, and the district chief of the Second District and the security squad leader and others gave gentle persuasion. At the same time, the Bureau of Social Affairs, together with the Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Party Department, dispatched personnel to discuss mediation measures. It was decided to telegram the factory's general manager, Lu Bohong, to go to the Bureau of Social Affairs for talks. Lu was ordered to go immediately, but was blocked by the workers, and some workers pushed a tramcar to the entrance of the factory, seemingly with a purpose. At that time, the security squad leader, Wu Liang, fearing that an incident would occur, personally stepped forward to stop them. While dispersing the crowd, there was a sudden boom, and Captain Wu's legs were injured. Two security soldiers, one police officer from the Second District, and ten workers were slightly injured in their feet, except for one person who was injured in the face. Captain Wu was not yet aware of his own injuries at the time and ordered the soldiers he brought to gather outside the factory to maintain order. The regiment headquarters, upon hearing the news, immediately dispatched two senior military officers to send Captain Wu and the injured soldiers to the regiment's medical treatment. In order to clarify responsibility, they immediately inspected the soldiers' guns at the scene, and there were no signs of gunfire. The bullets carried by each soldier, 26 in each row, were also complete and intact. Soon, the municipal government heard the news and sent personnel to the scene to investigate and sent the injured workers to Renji Hospital for treatment. According to the doctor's report, the injured had their wounds bandaged separately, and X-rays were taken to determine that the wounds were caused by small pieces scattered into the skin, which did not appear to be gunshot wounds and were not very serious. Except for one person who should be hospitalized for treatment, the rest had already returned on their own. After the Public Security Bureau's detailed investigation, it can be proven that this loud boom that injured more than ten people was definitely not caused by gunfire. Furthermore, according to the doctor's examination, the wounds were small pieces of metal, which seemed to be from a bomb. It is said that the Public Security Bureau is still continuing to investigate the source of this object and the person who used it.

Another report says that after the incident, the municipal government immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau and the Security Department to dispatch police teams to the city's water and electricity companies to provide effective protection, and ordered the Public Utilities Bureau to dispatch personnel to take care of the situation to ensure that the city's water and electricity supply would not be affected.

▲Mayor's Statement: Yesterday, after the bombing incident at the Chinese Business Electric Company, reporters rushed to the municipal government to inquire about Mayor Wu's attitude towards the case. He said that labor strikes at the factory have occurred for years, and although the Party and government agencies have repeatedly mediated and dealt with them, the strikes have risen and fallen from time to time, and have never been resolved. Today, the factory suddenly lost the tram car key, and the workers suddenly announced a strike, surrounding the company's manager, gathering crowds to coerce and refusing to be suppressed by the police, and throwing bombs to injure people while the security team leader was persuading them. It seems that this is not a simple labor dispute. There must be bad elements among the workers deliberately disrupting local order and social tranquility, and inciting unrest from within. In order to protect public safety and maintain the law, I have no choice but to thoroughly investigate and strictly pursue the matter in order to deter future offenders. Therefore, in addition to ordering the Public Utilities Bureau and the Public Security Bureau to find ways to effectively protect the factory's water and power generation, I have also ordered the Bureau of Social Affairs and the Public Security Bureau to work with the Party Department to severely investigate the situation that caused the disaster today.

However, according to another report, the Chinese Business Electric Company's workers demanded improvements to their treatment conditions. After the Municipal Party Department reviewed the matter, the Bureau of Social Affairs was working to mediate the situation. Yesterday, the workers in the vehicle department claimed that all the tram keys had been stolen, so the trams on all routes could not leave the factory. The Party and government agencies immediately dispatched personnel to investigate, temporarily dispatched police to strictly guard the area, and advised the workers to find a way to hand over the spare keys to the workers. However, the workers refused to work because the issue of pay raises had not been resolved, and went on strike. At 3:00 PM, the Bureau of Social Affairs convened a meeting to question them and again advised the union to no avail. At that time, the company's manager, Lu Bohong, was surrounded by workers in the factory. The security team, upon hearing the news, went to rescue him, but the workers prevented them from entering. At 3:30 PM, a hand grenade was suddenly thrown from the crowd, followed by the sound of gunfire, resulting in the injury of one security team platoon leader, three soldiers, and eleven workers. Qi Bingyuan, car driver No. 19, was injured in both feet and face; Chen Hongfan, ticket seller No. 15, was injured in his left leg; Zhu Shunquan, ticket seller No. 76, was injured in his left wrist; Qin Jiarong, ticket seller No. 7, was injured in his right leg; Hu Hengqing, car driver No. 22, was injured in his right foot; Wang Asi, engine room worker, was injured in his right leg, with a bullet entering his face and exiting through his mouth; Zhang Jiashu, ticket seller No. 57, was injured in his left leg; Li Fugen, car driver No. 23, was injured in his left leg; Wang Xiyuan, ticket seller No. 89, was injured in his left foot, face, and chest; and Hu Shuangfu, ticket seller No. 78, was injured in his left hand; Zhu Kaifa was injured in his left foot and right face. The injured workers were all transported to Renji Hospital by ambulance from the West District Fire Brigade. It is said that Wang Asi, the engine room worker who was seriously injured, may be in danger of death.

Bomb and Pistol Attack at Maotai Store 157

▲Two Youths Appear Suddenly

▲Warning Letter Sent a Month Ago

▲Customers Terrified

▲Wang Zhengtao Hit in the Waist

At 9:45 PM last night, while the Maotai Woolen Goods Store at 310 Xinzha Road was crowded with customers, two youths suddenly appeared outside. One was tall and the other short, both around twenty years old, wearing gray cloth robes. They each threw a bomb towards the glass counter at the entrance of the store. Upon seeing this, the customers were terrified and scrambled towards the street to escape. However, the bombs did not explode upon landing. The two youths then drew pistols and each fired a shot at the long glass counter beside the store. One bullet hit the lower glass pane of the counter, and the other struck Wang Zhengtao from Zhenjiang, the store's accountant, who was standing by the counter, in the left waist, causing him to immediately fall to the ground. Upon hearing the gunshots, nearby businesses were thrown into panic. The two youths then fled amidst the chaos. When the nearby patrol officers arrived, they found Wang unconscious and immediately reported to the police station. A large number of detectives were dispatched and first transported the injured Wang Zhengtao to Baolong Hospital for treatment. It is reported that the bullet is still in his abdomen and his life is still in danger. Afterwards, they inspected the scene and recovered a bullet head under the long glass counter, along with the two unexploded bombs, and took them to the police station for investigation. According to the store's staff, they had not received any letters or warnings prior to the incident, except for a warning letter received a month ago. They also said that the goods sold had been inspected.

Ministry of Communications Orders Recall of China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company Shares 158

▲Zhu Jia-hua Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Minister of Communications Zhu Jia-hua arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing at 8:00 AM yesterday. In addition to attending the meeting on the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund, he also met with acting President Song Ziwen and the directors and supervisors of the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company. It is heard that the Ministry of Communications is already discussing the method for recalling shares. Further news regarding the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company is detailed below.

▲Ministry of Communications Order: When reporters interviewed Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Communications yesterday to inquire about the method of recalling shares, Minister Zhu replied that the government's intention is that if shareholders are willing to hand over their shares to the government at the fixed price of fifty taels, the government will pay in cash; otherwise, they will not be forced. As for the date of the share recall and the entrusted organization, the Ministry has issued an order to the board of directors of the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company. The reporter also obtained a copy of the Ministry of Communications' order, which is transcribed below: "Order: Regarding the matter of the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company being nationalized, the National Government has issued a clear order. All shares should be submitted within a fixed period, from December 1, 1932 to December 28, 1933, to the Central Bank, which is entrusted to verify the shares and pay fifty taels of silver per share according to regulations. The detailed measures should be drafted and submitted to the board of directors for approval. This order."

▲Liu Hongsheng Speaks: A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency interviewed Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company, yesterday. According to his answers to the reporter's questions: (1) Minister Zhu came to Shanghai today, but I have not yet met him, so the follow-up matters of the company have not been discussed. (2) The implementation date for the share recall still needs to be approved by the Ministry of Communications. However, the measures reported in Nanjing in today's (18th) newspaper are not a formal draft decision. As far as I know, when the shares are recalled in the future, in addition to being recalled at the assessed price of fifty taels, if the shareholders do not want to sell, they will not be forced to sell, and it is hoped that they can be shareholders with the government. (3) Except for a letter of protest from the China Business Corporation on the day the four wharves were taken back, there has been no second letter. The company has not yet responded because the case has not been completely resolved.

▲Payment of Back Pay: Due to economic reasons during Li Guojie's tenure, the salaries of the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company employees have only been paid for half a month since September, and no payment was made at all in October. It is learned that the new General Manager Liu Hongsheng has already notified the accounting department that all back pay will be paid together with this month's salary starting from the end of this month.

▲Appointment of Secretaries: Since the reorganization of the bureau, the staff of each department has been fully announced. Yesterday, seven secretaries were officially appointed to the secretariat, namely Xu Zhiyi, Chen Yinfu, and Wu Dongqing as secretaries, and Wang Jianxun, Cai Lisheng, Jiang Shan, and Qi Fuming as assistant secretaries.

▲News from the Li Residence: Since Li Guojie was detained, his wife has been running around to find ways to rescue him, hoping that Li can regain his freedom as soon as possible. The afternoon before yesterday, Mrs. Li went to the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company to see General Manager Liu Hongsheng and asked him to find a way. Liu said that this was a government order and told her to see Song Ziwen, the acting President of the Executive Yuan. Mrs. Li then changed her route to the Song residence, but the outcome is still unknown.

▲Impeachment Proposal: Supervisor Li Menggeng discussed that Li Guojie's unauthorized pledge of company assets and loss of shipping administration, if not signed by Chen Fumu, may not be legally effective. Chen and others are suspected of colluding in fraud. The Supervisory Yuan has completed the review of the impeachment memorial and evidence and has sealed it and sent it to the President for review, and then requested the National Government to order the Committee on Disciplinary Punishment of Public Officials to punish them according to law.

▲Contract Losses: Gao Tingzi, Director of the Shipping Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications, discussed that there are many points in the contract for the pledge of funds by the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company that result in the loss of sovereignty. The most important are: (1) Although the contract is for a period of twenty years, the China Merchants' Steam Navigation Company has been losing money every year. How can such a huge amount of money be repaid? It is simply turning a small debtor into a large debtor and permanently forfeiting all assets to foreigners. Other losses such as the actual receipt of 85% and the amount of subsidiary funds are not worth mentioning. (2) According to the rights of the creditor, the mortgaged property can be re-mortgaged to a third party. If it is stipulated that in twenty years, if it is re-mortgaged for several years, even up to a hundred years, the debtor has no right to intervene. (3) In addition to the four wharves, there are also large areas of land among the mortgaged properties. The Shanghai market is developing rapidly. During this period, the company can build houses on the land. When we raise funds to recover the property in the future, if the company demands tens of millions of dollars for the cost of building on the land, how will we deal with it in the future? It will inevitably be permanently occupied by others.

Li Guojie's Illegal Signing of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Loan Contract in Full (Continued) 161

▲ Officially announced by the Ministry of Transportation on the 16th evening

Divided into ㈠ Contract ㈡ Memorandum ㈢ Lease ㈣ Mortgage Payment Contract, four parts

Lease agreement between China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (hereinafter referred to as "Lessor," which term shall include its successors, heirs, or representatives) and American-China Corporation (hereinafter referred to as "Lessee," which term shall include its successors, heirs, or representatives). The Lessor hereby leases the following wharves and real estate owned by it located on the west bank of the Huangpu River in Shanghai, in the International Settlement and the French Concession, and on the east bank of the Huangpu River in Pudong: A. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Central Wharf, i.e., American Registry Deed Nos. 463, 464, 467, 510, 465, 466, 509, and 511 (i.e., British Municipal Council Eastern District Land Registry No. 1), with a total land area of 24 mu, 8 fen, 7 li, 2 hao according to the deeds, plus an additional 4 mu, 4 fen, 1 li, 2 hao due after surtax, totaling a land area of 29 mu, 2 fen, 8 li, 4 hao, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the property; B. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company North Wharf, i.e., American Registry Nos. 461, 462, and British Registry Nos. 486, 607 (i.e., British Municipal Council Eastern District No. 1019), with a total land area of 74 mu, 7 fen, 7 li, 5 hao according to the deeds, plus an additional 21 mu, 6 fen, 5 li due after surtax, totaling a land area of 96 mu, 4 fen, 2 li, 5 hao, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the property; C. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company China Wharf, i.e., British Registry No. 12503, with a total land area of 189 mu, 7 fen, 5 li, 5 hao, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the property. The lease agreement was signed by both parties on September 6, 1932, as follows: 1. The Lessor hereby leases the above-mentioned three wharves and real estate (hereinafter referred to as "the Leased Wharves," which term shall include the land, buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures of each wharf) to the Lessee for a term of twenty years. Upon expiration of the term, the Lessee may continue the lease for another ten years. The term shall commence on November 1, 1932. The annual rent is set at 300,000 taels, payable in four installments per year, with each installment covering three months, i.e., January 31, April 30, July 31, and October 31 of each year. 2. Both parties mutually agree that the above-mentioned installments of rent shall be credited by the Lessee to the Lessor's account at each due date as part of the interest payable by the Lessor to the Lessee on the mortgage loan concluded by both parties on September 6, 1932. 3. Both parties agree that once the wharf company is established, the Lessor may, when the Lessee raises capital, join as a shareholder for half of the ordinary shares or any amount deemed appropriate. 4. The Lessee shall maintain the Leased Wharves in perfect condition at all times and shall pay all necessary maintenance and repair costs. 5. The Lessee shall insure the existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the Leased Wharves, as well as any buildings constructed or added on the Leased Wharves in the future, against fire and water damage for an appropriate amount during the lease term. In the event of fire or flood, the Lessee shall use the compensation received to rebuild or repair the premises, and shall pay any necessary expenses from its own funds to restore the Leased Wharves to their original perfect and solid condition. 6. The Lessor acknowledges that once the Lessee has paid the rent and complied with all the provisions of the contract, the Lessee shall enjoy the Leased Wharves without hindrance from the Lessor during the lease term, and shall not permit interference from any other person within the scope of the law. 7. The Lessee shall have full power to build or rebuild any type of building on any land of the property mentioned in this agreement that is not needed for its wharf business, and to lease it separately to others for use as offices, shops, residences, or other appropriate businesses. 8. The Lessee shall have the right

Page 14

to assign, transfer, or sublet the Leased Wharves to a third party, but the term shall not exceed the final expiry date stipulated in Article 1 of this lease. It may also sublet land not needed for the wharf business to a third party to establish a building construction agreement, the term of which shall also not exceed the final expiry date stipulated in this lease. In the event that the Lessee does not wish to comply with the provisions for continuation of this agreement on the expiry date of the twenty-year term, the Lessor shall accept the land lease and building construction agreement concluded by the Lessee with a third party which has not yet expired, and acknowledge all provisions of the agreement, continuing to comply with them until the expiry date of the agreement. 9. Both parties mutually acknowledge and agree that all buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, other structures, and all improvements, etc., added by the Lessee on any of the above-mentioned properties, whether for subletting or for the wharf business, shall be re-evaluated at the expiry of this lease, and the Lessee shall be reimbursed by the Lessor. 10. Both parties further acknowledge and agree that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company China Wharf mentioned in this lease refers to the entirety of the property. All buildings, wharves, pontoons, and other structures adjacent to the east of the China Wharf, which were previously leased by the Ocean Shipping Wharf Company, are also within this property, as the location of the former Ocean Shipping Wharf Company was actually the eastern part of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company China Wharf property. Both parties further acknowledge and agree that the easternmost real estate and wharf warehouses, etc., of the above-mentioned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company China Wharf are also included in this lease. The Lessor must recover the houses, warehouses, wharves, etc., previously leased by the Ocean Shipping Wharf Company from the Ministry of Transportation. 11. Both parties agree that, in addition to the land tax and grain tribute payable to the Chinese government, which shall be borne by the Lessor, all taxes and levies currently and in the future imposed on the Leased Wharves by the Public Concession Municipal Council, the Chinese government, or the Shanghai authorities shall be the responsibility of the Lessee and shall be paid by the Lessee. 12. Both parties agree that in the event that any part of the Leased Wharves is destroyed or damaged by storms, heavy rain, earthquakes, internal or external wars, and unavoidable natural disasters or man-made calamities, rendering the buildings unusable for the wharf business, the Lessee may, under such circumstances, suspend payment of the rent for the duration of the damage and during the reconstruction of the buildings. 13. The Lessee may have the riverbanks of the unrated Central and Northern Wharves rated according to the regulations of the Lingpu Engineering Bureau. The expenses required for the rating shall be separately recorded in the Lessor's arrears account. If the arrears are not repaid on time, the Lessee shall calculate interest at the usual annual rate of nine percent. Whenever the Lessor has funds to repay, the arrears shall be immediately deducted. 14. Both parties mutually acknowledge that from the date of signing the contract, any problems, disputes, or disagreements, and however they may arise, shall be immediately referred to two impartial persons. One impartial person shall be selected by the Lessor, and one shall be selected by the Lessee. If the two impartial persons cannot agree, the two impartial persons may jointly elect a chief impartial person. All must be judged in accordance with current American law. The result of the judgment, whether determined by the two impartial persons or by the chief impartial person, shall be acknowledged, obeyed, and willing to be implemented by both parties. If one party has notified the other party of the impartial person it has appointed, and the other party fails to appoint or refuses to appoint its due impartial person within ten days, then whatever the problem, dispute, or disagreement, the party that has already selected an impartial person may immediately submit it to the impartial person of that party for exclusive judgment. Both parties further acknowledge and agree that in all the above-mentioned circumstances, the result of the judgment of the impartial person appointed by that party shall be fully obeyed by that party and the other party, and the impartial person of that party shall be regarded as if appointed by agreement of both parties. 15. This lease is part of the contract signed on September 6, 1932, and is an appendix to that contract. This lease is attached to the end of that contract. Lease agreement made on September 6, 1932. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, witnessed by the Chairman of the Board of Directors of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, witnessed by the General Manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, witnessed by American-China Corporation. All of the above have been approved by the Supervisory Office of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company of the National Government's Ministry of Transportation. Printed by the Supervisory Office of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company of the Ministry of Transportation. (This is a translated copy, the English version is the original).

Contract made this sixth day of September, 1932, between the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (hereinafter referred to as "Party A," which term shall include its successors, heirs, or representatives) and American-China Corporation (hereinafter referred to as "Party B," which term shall include its successors, heirs, or representatives). Both parties have signed a mortgage loan of Shanghai Tael 10,000,000, and for the above-mentioned mortgage loan Party B is specially permitted to sell and issue bonds. The date, amount, and conditions for the payment of the mortgage loan are fully stated in this contract. Both parties agree to stipulate the terms as follows: 1. Party A is willing to fully hand over the real estate stated in the mortgage deed signed with Party B on September 6, 1932, to Party B as collateral for the bonds sold and issued as stated in this contract. The real estate in the above-mentioned mortgage deed is (A) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Central Wharf located along the Huangpu River in Hongkou, Shanghai International Settlement, i.e., American Registry Nos. 463, 464, 467, 510, 465, 466, 509, and 511. According to the deeds, the total land area is 24 mu, 8 fen, 7 li, 2 hao, plus an additional 4 mu, 4 fen, 1 li, 2 hao due under the surtax right, totaling 29 mu, 2 fen, 8 li, 4 hao, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the land; (B) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company North Wharf located along the Huangpu River in Hongkou, Shanghai International Settlement, i.e., American Registry Nos. 461, 462, British Registry Nos. 486, 607. According to the deeds, the total land area is 74 mu, 7 fen, 7 li, 5 hao, plus an additional 21 mu, 6 fen, 5 li due under the surtax right, totaling 96 mu, 4 fen, 2 li, 5 hao, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the land; (C) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company China Wharf located along the Huangpu River in Pudong, Shanghai, i.e., British Registry No. 12503. According to the deeds, the total land area is 189 mu, 7 fen, 5 li, 5 hao. All properties to the east of the China Wharf that were once leased to the Ocean Shipping Wharf Company are also included, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the land; (D) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Yangjiadu Wharf located along the Huangpu River in Pudong, Shanghai, i.e., British Registry Nos. 723, 2115, and Shanghai County Deeds Nos. 3, 150, and 155. According to the deeds and deeds, the total land area is 120 mu, 1 fen, 2 li, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the land; (E) China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Jinliyuan Wharf located along the Huangpu River in the French Concession, i.e., (1) French Municipal Council Land Registry Nos. 50A, 51A, 52A, 54A, 55A, 56A, 57A, 58A, 59A, 64A, 64B, 59A, and 75 Inside. The above properties are all east of the tramway and along the Huangpu River. There are also the eastern halves of Nos. 51 and 64, and No. 75. The above properties are west of the tramway. According to the French Municipal Council Land Registry, the total land area is 33 mu, 9 fen, 1 li, 4 hao, 7 si, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, wharves, pontoons, and other structures on the land; 2. French Municipal Council Land Registry Nos. 50, 52, 54, 55, 56, 57, 58, 59, 60, and the western half of No. 64. The above properties are all west of the tramway. According to the French Municipal Council Land Registry, the total land area is 29 mu, 6 fen, 4 li, 7 hao, 3 si. The above nine and a half plots of French Registry land belong to the Ji Yu Real Estate Co., Ltd. The company has fully approved the inclusion of the above-mentioned real estate belonging to the company in the above-mentioned mortgage deed as collateral. This has been acknowledged by the company's board of directors and separately signed and sealed by the chairman of the board at the end of this contract and this mortgage deed, together with all existing buildings, warehouses, and other structures on the land. 2. Both parties mutually acknowledge that for the purpose of raising the above-mentioned mortgage loan, Party B may use the various properties listed in the above-mentioned mortgage deed as collateral, and issue bonds with a total face value of Shanghai Tael 10,000,000 in the name of Party B or in the name designated by Party B, with a term of twenty years, at a discounted price of 85%. The issued bonds shall be completely separate from the bonds that Party B or its designee has already issued or will issue in the future, so as to be recognized. 3. Both parties agree that Party A shall pay Party B interest on this mortgage loan at an annual rate of 9%, calculated on the face value of the issued bonds. Each bond shall accrue interest from the date of sale. The interest payment period shall be every three months. Interest not paid when due shall also accrue compound interest at the usual annual rate of 9%. 4. Both parties mutually acknowledge and agree that the amount of discount and the amount of interest, whether profit or loss, between this mortgage loan and the sale and issuance of bonds are the responsibility of Party B and have nothing to do with Party A. 5. After this contract and the mortgage deed mentioned in this contract are formally signed by both parties, Party B shall, in accordance with the discounted price and all provisions stated in this contract, issue bonds with a face value of Shanghai Tael 10,000,000 to meet the following needs of Party A: (1) To pay off the principal of the HSBC Bank real estate mortgage loan of 5,000,000 taels and the interest payable; (2) To pay off the principal and interest of the S德堂 real estate mortgage loan of 200,000 taels; (3) To pay Party B 2.5% calculated on the total face value of the issued bonds; (4) If there is any surplus, it shall be credited to Party A's account for Party A to pay off other arrears or for Party B's business needs. 6. Party A, for the above-mentioned mortgage loan represented by the total face value of the issued bonds, permits Party B to lease the wharves and real estate of Party A, B, and C as stated in Article 1 of this contract, starting from November 1 of this year for a term of twenty years, which may be extended for another ten years upon expiration. The annual rent is set at 300,000 taels, payable in four installments per year, with each installment covering three months. The terms and provisions of the lease of the three wharves shall be stipulated in a separate contract. 7. In order to prepare for the payment of the interest on this mortgage loan and to annually raise funds to be deposited into the sinking fund account for the repayment of the bond loan, Party A designates the following income for the above-mentioned purposes: (A) The annual rent of the Central, Northern, and China Wharves leased to Party B; (B) The rent receivable for the various properties listed in Section 2, Item E, of Article 1 of this contract (It is noted that this rent cannot be collected at present and will have to wait until the end of this year, when Party A cancels the mortgage loan contract and the land lease building contract, etc., signed between the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the 久昌 Company, before it can be implemented); (C) 25% of the net profit of Party A in the shipping business shall be allocated each year; (D) Party B shall collect the wharf fees and warehouse rents, etc., that Party A should have on Jinliyuan and Yangjiadu on schedule. All additional expenses incurred by Party B in collecting these wharf fees and warehouse rents, etc., from Party A shall be borne by Party A. If practically needed, Party B may hire wharf and warehouse managers on its own, and the monthly salaries of these employees shall be borne by Party A. 8. All income under the above items shall be collected by Party B in its capacity. This income shall first be used to pay off the interest on this mortgage loan stipulated in this contract. If the rental income and all payments received are insufficient to pay off the interest on this mortgage loan stipulated in this contract, the interest that should have been paid but was not shall be recorded separately in Party A's arrears account as outstanding interest. The outstanding interest shall also accrue compound interest at the usual annual rate of 9%. If there is a surplus from the above-mentioned income items or if there are funds available from other sources, it shall be immediately credited to Party A's sinking fund account for repayment of the bonds to prepare for the payment of the principal of this mortgage loan sold and issued under this contract, and the interest due on this mortgage loan until the due date. Party B shall do its best to ensure that the funds in this income sinking fund account can be used to generate the maximum possible interest. The maximum interest earned must also be credited to the sinking fund account for repayment of the bond loan. The amount already credited to Party A's sinking fund account for repayment of the bond loan shall be managed entirely by Party B, but if Party A has a good plan to enable this sinking fund to generate a higher rate of interest, it may make a suggestion to Party B. 9. Party A acknowledges that during the term of this contract, it shall pay Party B a handling fee of 5% based on the amount of the above-mentioned income collected by Party B on its behalf, excluding the annual rent of the three wharves. All management and other services for the various houses or warehouses stated in Section 2, Item E, of Article 1 of this contract shall be borne by Party B. 10. Party A acknowledges that it shall pay Party B a commission of 2.5% calculated on the face value of the bonds issued under this contract. This commission shall be paid on the date of sale of each bond. 11. Party B agrees to completely separate the various receipts and payments accounts under this contract from Party B's own business accounts. 12. Party A acknowledges and agrees that none of the wharves, warehouses, and other real estate listed in this contract shall be mortgaged again, and guarantees to be responsible for handling all negotiations to eliminate any legal interference. If there have been negotiations for a second secured loan using the property as collateral, Party A shall be responsible for handling the matter clearly and shall not involve Party B. 13. Both parties understand and agree that in the event that Party A wishes to sell all or part of the above-mentioned properties during the term of this contract before this mortgage loan has been repaid, Party B shall have the right of first refusal to purchase all or part of the properties. Both parties agree that whether the sale is handled by Party A or by Party B, Party B shall be paid a normal commission of 2.5%. 14. In the event that Party A fails to repay the principal due on the date of maturity of this mortgage loan represented by the face value of the issued bonds and the interest payable on this mortgage loan according to the face value of the bonds, or the funds in Party A's sinking fund account for repayment of the bond loan are insufficient to repay all or part of the principal due on the date of maturity of the above-mentioned mortgage loan represented by the face value of the issued bonds and the interest payable on this mortgage loan according to the face value of the bonds, Party B shall have full power to dispose of or sell all or part of the properties listed in this contract by public auction or private negotiation to repay the principal and interest due. If it is still insufficient, Party A shall compensate by other means. If there is a surplus, Party B shall pay it to Party A after repaying the principal and interest due. 15. Party B acknowledges that once the principal, other payments, and commissions, etc., for the bonds issued under this contract have been fully repaid, all the real estate listed in this contract shall be re-transferred to Party A by Party B. 16. Both parties mutually acknowledge that from the date of signing this contract, any problems, disputes, or disagreements, and however they may arise, shall be immediately referred to two impartial persons. One impartial person shall be selected by Party A, and one shall be selected by Party B. If the two impartial persons cannot agree, the two impartial persons may jointly elect a chief impartial person. All must be judged in accordance with current American law. The result of the judgment, whether determined by the two impartial persons or by the chief impartial person, shall be acknowledged, obeyed, and willing to be implemented by both parties. If one party has notified the other party of the impartial person it has appointed, and the other party fails to appoint or refuses to appoint its due impartial person within ten days, then whatever the problem, dispute, or disagreement, the party that has already selected an impartial person may immediately submit it to the impartial person of that party for exclusive judgment. Both parties further acknowledge and agree that in all the above-mentioned circumstances, the result of the judgment of the impartial person appointed by that party shall be fully obeyed by that party and the other party, and the impartial person of that party shall be regarded as if appointed by agreement of both parties. 17. This contract is part of this mortgage deed and lease agreement, and is an appendix to this mortgage deed and lease agreement. Contract made on September 6, 1932. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, witnessed by the Chairman of the Board of Directors of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, witnessed by the General Manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, witnessed by the Chairman of the Board of Directors of Ji Yu Real Estate Co., Ltd., witnessed by American-China Corporation. All of the above have been approved by the Supervisory Office of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company of the National Government's Ministry of Transportation. Printed by the Supervisory Office of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company of the Ministry of Transportation. (This is a translated copy, the English version is the original).

The Shanghai Chinese National Coal Production and Sales Joint Association was originally a national coal production and sales joint agency. A Strong Effort to Oppose Telephone Rate Hikes, Documents and Telegrams 165

▲ The Shanghai Municipal District Association and the Nanjing Road Business Community Association, in order to oppose telephone rate increases, sent a telegram to various ministries and institutes in the capital, Nanjing, addressed to the National Government of Nanjing, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Ministry of Industry: This time, the Shanghai Telephone Company first obtained approval from the Engineering Bureau of the First Special District, and then the consent of the Board of Directors of the Second Special District, to increase residential telephone fees from 52 taels of silver to 65 taels, and business fees from 78 taels of silver to 105 taels, and to increase the charge per call from 5 fen (small coin) to 4 fen of silver, and to retroactively apply this from March 27th of this year. While we recognize that, in reality, the telephone company may inevitably obtain the approval of the authorities within the district through coercive and intimidating means such as disconnecting lines, and while we may not be able to achieve the goal of canceling the rate increase and its retroactive application, we will not abandon our interests, so that this unjust and barbaric method may be subjected to the judgment of world opinion. Telephones are a public utility. On the one hand, they obtain a patent; on the other hand, due to low usage fees, the business, because of the patent, consolidates its capital interests. It should therefore be lower than the general business. Checking this year's discount rate of the US Federal Reserve Bank is 2.5%, the Bank of England in the UK is 2%, and the interest rate on Chinese government bonds is 6%. The interest rates on the corporate bonds of the Shanghai Electric Power Company and the Shanghai Telephone Company are both 6%. We do not know for what reason the municipal authorities within the district approved the Shanghai Telephone Company's revenue to be 8%, plus another 2%, totaling 10%, thus increasing the burden on users. The Engineering Bureau, which first approved this method, has already failed in its responsibility to those it represents. Even if we concede that the current telephone fee increase is constrained by the contract signed between the Engineering Bureau and the Shanghai Telephone Company on August 5, 1930, the price increase must be in accordance with the report of Mr. An Mei. The contract does not stipulate that its basis can be the unreasonable 10% interest. Investigating the capital invested by the Shanghai Telephone Company and the total number of telephone lines and equipment it has prepared, there are tens of thousands of households, of which tens of thousands have been used. Assuming the latter is 30,000 households and the former is 100,000 households, then the capital used for the 70,000 unused telephone lines and equipment is due to the company's miscalculation and self-inflicted stagnation, which has nothing to do with the users. Why must the Engineering Bureau force the users to bear the interest on the capital that has been left idle due to the company's miscalculation? The most unfair thing this time is that the obligations of the telephone company under the contract are exempted and fulfilled as much as possible, and the rights are protected as much as possible, while the economic decline suffered by the taxpayers it represents after the Japanese disturbance in Shanghai is ignored. It is unwilling to exempt them from their forced obligations and protect their right to low usage fees. This is the dereliction of duty of the Director-General of the Engineering Bureau. The October 21st issue of the Engineering Bureau Gazette published a letter from Mr. Anson to Mr. Jones, the Director-General of the Public Concession, regarding his opinion on telephone rate increases. From the meaning of the third paragraph of Mr. Anson's letter, Mr. An has already realized that it is difficult to escape the judgment of public opinion, and admits that this opinion does not take into account the changes in the economic situation during this period. It also says that if he were to be asked to come to China again to investigate, he would definitely have another report. This is sufficient to show that Mr. An's previous report admitted that he could not take into account the interests of the majority of the public at present, which led to disputes. The Engineering Bureau should also eliminate its prejudices, be responsible for negotiating with the company to cancel the compensation for the new price, set a fair price, and obtain the consent of the users to implement it on a regular basis to eliminate disputes and achieve a peaceful solution. We earnestly request your department to immediately lodge a serious protest with the diplomatic missions to strive for a fair solution that takes into account the interests of both parties. We cannot express our prayers enough. The Shanghai Municipal District Association and the Nanjing Road Business Community Association respectfully request.

▲ The Nanjing Road Business Community Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens' Association, in order to strongly oppose the telephone rate increase, yesterday again submitted a document to the Municipal Government, stating: The Shanghai Telephone Company rashly stopped telephone service, and negotiations are becoming increasingly tense. Please quickly correct this to reduce the burden on the citizens and find ways to stop illegal actions and stabilize business affairs. The association previously reported that the Shanghai Telephone Company illegally increased rates and requested your government to quickly negotiate with the Engineering Bureau and telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to request a serious protest to the diplomatic missions. Later, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent a telegram stating: "Your telegram has been received. If the Shanghai Concession's telephone rate increase is as stated in your telegram, then the company's measures are indeed inappropriate and should be corrected to reduce the burden on the citizens. The Shanghai Municipal Government has been instructed to investigate and handle the matter. A special reply from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has been printed and distributed." However, the company still adheres to its fixed opinion on the rate increase and refuses to yield. It even intensifies its coercion by disconnecting lines and doing whatever it wants to achieve its goals. Moreover, it was reported that on November 13, more than 500 users were disconnected. All users in the city are indignant, and the incident is expanding and becoming increasingly tense. We sincerely fear that delays and a failure to stop this will not only increase the accidental losses of the citizens, but also lead to an unsustainable state of social unrest. The future is worrying. Therefore, we submit another document requesting your government to examine and approve it, quickly investigate and handle it in accordance with the deleted telegram, and stop the company's illegal actions for the public convenience.

Various Organizations Petition for Rent Reduction 166

▲ Document Addressed to Party and Government Organs

▲ The Hongkou Various Organizations Citizens' Association, the Hongkou Various District Branches, and the Yuanyang Road, Dongyouheng Road, Hanbury Road, East and West Huade Road, Broadway Road, Haining Road, North Jiangxi Road, Suzhou Road, North Shanxi Road, Jiaxing Road, Wuzhou Road, Zhoujiazui Road, Yuezhou Road, Tongzhou Road, Airange Road, Kenenghai Road, Yinxian Road, Yangshupu Road, and other Business Community Associations and other organizations yesterday specially convened a joint representative meeting. After the meeting, a document was submitted to the Municipal Government, stating: In order to reduce and exempt rent and relieve people's livelihood, we respectfully request your review and arbitration. The member stores at the end of North Jiangxi Road, such as Xinkai Road, Member Stores, Zida Changdahong Building, and other 50 households, jointly stated that Fanzhi was promoted to Rong Sheng Gengfu Sanli, which is the property of Xielong Real Estate Company. The houses were newly built and completed not long ago, and the road in that area was opened last year and has not yet been completed, resulting in a lack of pedestrian traffic in the market there. Moreover, the area was particularly dangerous during the January 28th Incident. The state after the war is comparable to the horror during the war. In such a harsh environment, the market is declining, and it is conceivable that the citizens who want to live there did not move in until September. Even today, the houses are empty and sparsely populated, extremely desolate, and the rent is high, and the small rents are as high as three months, which is an evil example of opening a rental house that violates the decrees of our government. Now, all the tenants are united in demanding a 30% rent reduction, the return of small rents, and the relief of the market. The rent price of a landlord renting out a house should be based on the situation, and it should not only seek profit and increase the burden on ordinary small businesses. The market in that area is declining, and the smoke and fire are sparse, which is indeed vastly different from other prosperous places. Rent reduction is a fair demand of the citizens to maintain people's livelihood and show compassion for business difficulties. It is reasonable to submit a document requesting a review and prompt arbitration to avoid disputes for the public convenience.

▲ Citizens' Association The Citizens' Association yesterday submitted a document to the Municipal Party Headquarters for the rent reduction movement, stating: Respectfully submitted, according to the letters from the 20 district branches of our association, since the rent reduction movement in our city has been going on for a long time, a satisfactory solution has not been seen. Although the Municipal Party Headquarters, etc., previously submitted a request to the National Government to send personnel to Shanghai to consider the situation and revise the rent exemption standards, several months have passed and it has not been implemented. Since the January 28th Incident occurred in our city, our industrial and commercial sectors have been completely destroyed, and the damage suffered is incalculable. Although the Municipal Government has announced rent exemption standards for areas such as Zhabei and Nanshi, the central area south of the Suzhou River has been ignored and no mention has been made of it. The bead is in arrears and the balance is not restored. Although the merchants in our central district were not directly ravaged by the violent bandits, the two-month strike and the stagnation of commerce have caused great losses in operating expenses, which cannot be overstated. Moreover, the central district is commercially prosperous and densely populated, and the demand for rent is greater than the supply, so the rent price is increasing day by day. Furthermore, the operation of wealthy merchants is monopolized, which makes the land price rise day by day and the rent more expensive. The rent alone accounts for more than half of the expenses of a store. Can it be said that the current demand for reduction and exemption is excessive? However, if this continues without a resolution, disputes will arise repeatedly, which is ultimately not a good strategy. In recent days, our association has been criticized and urged by members to resolve the issue, making it difficult for us to remain silent. Correspondingly, we have recorded the case and forwarded it to you, hoping that you will examine it, handle it, and avoid disputes while maintaining commerce, and give us a reply so that we can follow it. This is our prayer, and it is truly convenient for the Party to resolve the suffering of the tenants as soon as possible.

The Bao Da Silk Factory Case Settled 169

▲ Travel Expenses Issued by Creditors for Dismissal

Since the January 28th Incident, Tianbao Road Bao Da Silk Weaving Factory immediately announced the closure and liquidation of all workers. After the order was restored, it presented a request to the Party and government agencies for relief because the factory owner refused to meet and could not proceed. The labor union issued a warning to the factory owner in the newspaper. Recently, the factory leased out and started work, refusing to hire old workers. The Social Affairs Bureau specially convened the creditors of the Da Silk Factory, the representative of Liugongji, Lian Shoushan, and the factory owner of Dachangde, Cheng Wuting, yesterday, along with the seventh district silk weaving labor union Zheng Lili and Qing Han, to mediate. The mediation was recorded by the mediators Zhu Guilin and Wang Zuofang, and the two sides agreed to resolve the issue. After the Bao Da Silk Factory closed down, travel expenses totaling $180 were issued by the creditors of Liugongji to dismiss the workers.

Tian Lun Silk Weaving Factory Resumes Work 170

▲ Working in Shifts at Specified Times

After the Tian Lun Silk Weaving Factory in Mingyuanfang, Huade Road, stopped the night shift the day before yesterday, the day and night shift workers competed for work, resulting in a conflict. The factory immediately announced a shutdown. The Social Affairs Bureau convened both labor and management at 10:00 AM yesterday for mediation. Fang Dehua of the Tian Lun Silk Weaving Factory and Wei Shouchang and Shao Hongqin of the fourth district silk weaving labor union were present. The meeting was chaired by Tan Peiyan of the Social Affairs Bureau. First, the labor and management representatives stated the process, and then they discussed and agreed to sign a reconciliation record: (1) The factory stipulates that work is for 16 hours in two shifts; (2) The wages remain the same at 3.6%; (3) Those who resume work for more than three days will be given a food allowance of $0.20 per person per day by the factory (this allowance will be stopped when the day and night shifts are resumed). As a result, all the workers entered the factory at the same time in the afternoon to work in shifts as usual.

Workers of Da China Welfare Rubber Shoe Factory Went on Strike Yesterday Morning 171

▲ Demanding Improved Treatment and Opposing the Dismissal of Representatives

▲ Party and Government Agencies Sent Personnel to Investigate Thoroughly and Find Ways to Mediate

The entire workforce of the Da China Welfare Rubber Shoe Factory in Xingjiazai Road, Zhabei, demanded improved treatment and opposed the factory's dismissal of worker representatives Zhu Caixing and others. They went on strike starting yesterday morning and went to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau to petition. At 3:00 PM, party and government agencies sent personnel to investigate thoroughly.

▲ Yesterday morning's strike. The factory was affected by the January 28th Incident and slightly reduced workers' wages to maintain the status quo when it resumed operations on April 1st of this year. On the 5th of this month, all workers demanded a restoration, which led to a strike. After the Wang Patrol Officer of the First Branch of the Fifth District persuaded them, they resumed work. The day before yesterday, factory director Yang Yongnian announced the dismissal of workers Zhu Caixing, Cai Geng, Li Rongchang, Qian Maotou, and other four people who had been absent from work without permission for more than three days, which aroused the workers' anger and led to a strike yesterday morning.

▲ Workers petition. After the factory's more than 400 male and female workers went on strike, they sent representatives from various departments to the Social Affairs Bureau to petition. The director of the Mediation Section, Wang Guangqing, met with them and ordered them to resume work immediately and wait for mediation. The Municipal Party Headquarters was met by Zhao Zhenhui of the Civil Training Section, who promised to work with the Social Affairs Bureau to find a way to mediate. At the same time, the First Branch of the Fifth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent police officers to be stationed near the factory to prevent any disturbances.

▲ Party and government investigation. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau sent Tan Peiyan to investigate the truth at 3:00 PM yesterday in order to verify and handle the matter.

French Concession Cracks Down on Brothels and Private Detective Agencies, and Employment Agencies 172

The French Consul General in Shanghai, Consul General Mei, recently issued new regulations cracking down on brothels, private detectives, and employment agencies in the concession. Excerpts are as follows: (1) Regulations on the Prohibition of Brothels (1) All brothels are strictly prohibited from employing or soliciting prostitutes suffering from infectious diseases (2) The Commissioner of Police may send personnel to enter all brothels at any time to conduct health inspections of prostitutes (3) Any prostitute who is found to be suffering from an infectious disease will have her permit revoked and the brothel owner will be punished by the Police Department. A fine of five to fifty yuan will be imposed for each sick prostitute found. In case of repeated offenses, the Police Department will be ordered by the French Consul General in Shanghai to close the brothel. (2) Regulations on the Prohibition of Private Detectives (1) No one may establish or operate a private detective agency in the French Concession without the approval of the French Consul General (2) Anyone who violates this order shall be subject to a fine of one to one hundred yuan (3) Regulations on Employment Agencies (1) No one may establish or operate an employment agency in the French Concession without the approval of the French Consul General (2) Anyone who violates this order shall be subject to a fine of one to one hundred yuan.
