Local News Two

Municipal Government to Host Visit to the City Center Today 173

▲ The Municipal Government Building Imitates the Ancient Palace Style

▲ Expected to be Completed by May or June Next Year

Construction of the city center area of the Greater Shanghai Plan has been underway for a long time. Construction of the Municipal Government Building and road projects in the area are currently being accelerated. It is expected that all projects will be completed by the end of June next year, and the Municipal Government will move to the area to work to promote the revitalization of the area. As for the first and second land acquisitions in the area, the first was delayed due to the impact of the Shanghai War. Now that the construction in the area has returned to its original state, those who pay the acquisition fee are very enthusiastic. In order to make all sectors understand, the Municipal Government has set up an invitation to visit this afternoon. The following is an exploration of the construction projects and the land acquisition fee collection by the Land Bureau.

▲ Road Engineering The roads in the city center area, such as Sanmin Road and Wuquan Road, have long been completed. The remaining roads have been delayed due to the impact of the Shanghai War. Now, because the Municipal Government Building is scheduled to be completed by the end of May next year, the road construction is being rushed. The road surfaces have been opened and leveled. The second step of the project is paving the road surface, which is also being actively carried out.

▲ Municipal Government Building The Municipal Government Building is located in the center of the city center area. The project started on June 1 last year, and the foundation stone laying ceremony was held on July 7. The entire project was contracted by Zhu Senji for a total of 550,000 yuan. It was originally scheduled to be completed by the end of this year. After the start of construction, the work was very smooth. However, the Shanghai War broke out in January of this year, and the project was suspended. The project was resumed on July 1 of this year, with a total suspension of five months, which resulted in the failure to complete the entire project on time. The contractor negotiated with the Municipal Government and agreed to extend the deadline to May of the following year. According to the construction foreman, the work is now very tight, with about 400 workers. Therefore, it will be completed by the end of June at the latest. The one-month delay is actually due to the large scale of the project and unforeseen circumstances. As for the losses suffered during the five-month suspension, the amount is small, about eight or nine thousand yuan. The Municipal Government did not recognize it and could not be compensated for it, so it can only be recognized as a loss.

▲ Current Status of the Project The construction of the Municipal Government Building is purely imitative of the palace style of our country, with a height of four floors. The large auditorium is on the second floor, high and spacious, and can accommodate hundreds of people. In front is a platform connected by stone steps, which can be used to go up and down. The cement walls, floors, and stone steps of the entire building are roughly in place. Water pipes and water heating pipes have also been installed. The work to be done in the future will be whitewashing, painting, and laying marble floors. The roof is currently using water along the bottom and will be paved with green glazed tiles produced in Guangdong in the future. The roof ridge will be decorated with roof ornaments. The interior will be painted with colored lacquer. In the future, after completion, the building with carved beams will be extremely beautiful.

▲ Distribution of Rooms The allocation of the Municipal Government offices was decided when the Municipal Government drew up the plans. The center of the ground floor is the entrance hall with two stone stairs and two elevators on the left and right. The east room is the dining room, the west room is the printing office and the first department office. Another room behind the entrance hall is for storage. The walls are made of cement and are specially thickened. The center of the second floor is the auditorium, the east is the conference room, and the west is the library. The east of the third floor is the office of the fourth and fifth departments, the west is the office of the second and third departments, and the middle facing south is the mayor's office, and the north is the reception room, with a corridor in the middle. The roof of the middle room on the fourth floor is higher for the dormitory, and the two sides are lower for use as a vault and storage room. The roof beams are fully exposed to allow air circulation.

▲ Building for each Bureau After the completion of the Municipal Government Building, it must be moved to, and the subordinate bureaus will also be gathered in one place to avoid the labor of going back and forth. However, the municipal treasury is insufficient, and the building expenses for each bureau are not easy to raise for a while. Therefore, it is decided to build temporary offices for the time being. Bids will be solicited for construction within two weeks, and construction will begin on the same day to complete the Municipal Government Building at the same time.

▲ Urgent Payment of Acquisition Fees The land acquisition fees in the city center area have been repeatedly urged by the Municipal Government. The first and second land acquisition fees total about 2 million yuan, which are paid in two installments. The first installment of about 1.5 million yuan is scheduled to be paid by the end of this year, and the second installment of about 500,000 yuan is due by the end of February next year. According to reporters' investigation at the Land Bureau yesterday, those who paid the fee in recent days were quite enthusiastic and have already obtained more than half of the amount.

▲ Municipal Government Reception In order to make all sectors understand the recent situation of the construction in the area, the Municipal Government specially invited all sectors to visit this afternoon and ordered the Public Works Bureau to prepare vehicles for the public to ride in.

Illegal Closure of the Moye Daily in Taicang 174

▲ The District Court Opened a Collegial Panel Yesterday

▲ Zhu Tieying Elaborated on the Process

▲ The Magistrate of Taicang County Will Be Summoned for Interrogation

The editor of the Moye Daily in Taicang, Zhu Tieying, offended the director of the Bureau of Business Tax, Hu Jiacong, because of business tax matters. The magistrate of Taicang County, Zhao Enju, sentenced him to one year of imprisonment, a fine of 200 yuan, and the closure of the newspaper. Zhu believed that this judgment not only confused the legal system, but also only transmitted the order to the government by hand, without adding a public trial to determine the sentence. Moreover, what was stated was all the truth, which was considered illegal. Therefore, he filed an appeal to the Shanghai District Court. After being tried, the presiding judge Qian Chengjun, along with judges Shen Youqi and Guan Liting, opened a collegial panel in the first court at 11:00 AM yesterday to first hear the appellant for refusing to accept the one-year imprisonment and a fine of 200 yuan. He asked when the Moye Daily was established. The reply was September 1928. He asked when the Business Tax Bureau was established in Taicang. The reply was 1930. He asked whether the Business Tax Bureau was under the jurisdiction of the provincial government. The reply was yes. He asked who the director was. The reply was Hu Jiacong. He asked who the author of the manuscript published on newspaper No. 157 was. The reply was the reporter Shuang Fengqing, whose name was Shuang Feng. He asked whether the collection of southern goods stores and rice shops mentioned in the newspaper was in Shuangfeng. The reply was yes. Shuangfeng is under the jurisdiction of the Eighth District. He asked whether the area was a war zone. The reply was no. He asked whether the Tax Bureau went to the area to collect money. The reply was yes. Although the area was not a war zone, it was greatly affected. He asked why the report was published if it was not a war zone. The reply was that at the provincial government meeting on August 9, Shu Shifu, the director of the Department of Finance, proposed that those in the direct war zone be exempt from the business tax for the whole year and the autumn and winter seasons of the previous year, and those who were affected be exempt from the spring and summer seasons of this year. He asked when the report was published. The reply was the newspaper of August 19. He asked when they collected the tax. It was not published in the newspaper. The reply was before August 19. How did they ask for correction but did not correct it? The reply was that because it was a fact, it was not necessary to correct it according to the publication law. However, it was of course close to stealing a chicken to collect it again after the exemption. At this point, Zhang Jingcheng, a resident of Wuxing, testified as the director of the Jiading Office of the Taicang Business Tax Bureau. The head office was in Taicang. He asked whether the bureau had received an order from the provincial government exempting the business tax when collecting it before. The reply was no, until August 25, when it was received and submitted. He asked when the Department of Finance issued the document. The reply was unknown. He asked who went to Shuangfeng Town to collect the tax. The reply was Zhu Jinjiang and Hu Derong. He asked when it was. The reply was August 15. He asked what season the tax collected in Shuangfeng Town was for. The reply was spring. He asked whether there were any inappropriate places in the tax collection office. The reply was that there must be some discrepancies. He asked why Zhu Tieying was charged. The reply was that he destroyed our reputation, and we did not do anything close to stealing chickens. We reported to the Department of Finance in advance on the day of collection. He asked whether the spring tax was returned later. The reply was that it was returned in the autumn, from September 1 to 30. At this point, the lawyer declared that Zhao Enju, as the supervisor, had a great relationship with the business tax and should be summoned for questioning. At this point, the judge said that there were still many witnesses to be summoned for continued interrogation.

Li Chuanting, Comprador of Dingsheng, Escapes Danger 175

▲ Fire Consumes Bandit Lair, People Plead for Mercy

▲ Bandit Leader Surrenders, Discarding Twin Pistols

▲ Li Chuanting Falls Ill in Bandit Lair

▲ Many Hostages Rescued Simultaneously

Li Chuanting, comprador of the Jardine Matheson & Co.'s Beiyang steamer "Dingsheng," was kidnapped by bandits in Tanggu for more than two months before finally being rescued recently. The matter was quite convoluted and truly worthy of record. The circumstances are investigated and noted as follows:

▲ North China Bandits Li Chuanting Kidnapped After Li Chuanting was kidnapped by bandits, the British Consul in Tianjin repeatedly requested the Tianjin authorities to rescue him, but there was no progress at first. Later, after purchasing information and investigating, it was discovered that Li was kidnapped by a major bandit group in North China and hidden in a fortress in Xin Village, more than forty miles from Tanggu. The area was the bandit lair, surrounded by fortifications that were difficult to attack. The bandit leader, named Liu Santaishi, was a young man with many followers and a large force. The surrounding villages were all under the control of the bandit. After Li was kidnapped, the government troops pursued him very closely, and he was unable to contact the hostage's family.

▲ Dispatching Troops to Suppress After the authorities obtained information, they immediately dispatched a regiment of troops to the bandit lair to suppress them. Unexpectedly, the bandit crowd came out to resist, and the bandit leader Liu Santaishi was able to fire guns with both hands, hitting the target every time. The government troops' attack failed to break through. Finally, they used the method of setting fire to burn down the bandit lair. This matter happened within the past week. The fire burned for many days, and the villages around the bandit lair were completely destroyed. The villagers in the same village suffered this disaster and knelt down to plead with the bandit leader.

▲ Bandit Leader Surrenders The villagers of the village went to Liu Santaishi to kneel and plead, saying that the entire fortress had been burned, which would cause too much damage. As a result, innocent people were implicated and too many were killed or injured, and they still could not escape. They requested that he not resist the government troops. The bandit leader, yielding to the request of the people, threw down his twin pistols and surrendered to the army, willing to be brought to justice and punished. Liu Santaishi was then captured. The army put out the fire and entered the village, arresting the bandit leader's brother and escorting them to Tianjin.

▲ Hostages Rescued A total of more than forty hostages were rescued from the bandit lair, including Li Chuanting. Most of the hostages were wealthy merchants and gentry. Li had become ill and was taken to Tianjin by the army. Upon receiving a telegram from Tianjin informing them that Li had been rescued by the government troops, his wife took a boat to Tianjin yesterday to welcome Li back to Shanghai for medical treatment in the hospital. They also reported the case to the British Consul, stating that the case had been solved. As for the bandit leader Liu Santaishi, according to the telegram, he was executed after arriving in Tianjin the day before yesterday.

Half a Card as Proof of Ransom 176

▲ Mistaking Detective for Client

▲ Tian Xinsong Highly Suspicious

Wang Youshan, a Chinese detective of the Shanghai Municipal Council Detective Branch, was walking near the intersection of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road at about 8:00 AM the day before yesterday when a man wearing a green cotton robe and a black vest stepped forward and asked Wang if his name was Li Jinshan. Wang, thinking that he came abruptly, casually replied that he was and asked the man what was the matter. The man immediately showed half a card printed with the name of Li Jinshan, saying that he had come to negotiate the ransom. Wang suspected his behavior and took him to the detective office for interrogation. According to the man's initial statement, his name was Tang Zhaonian, but then he suddenly said his name was Tian Xinsong, from Suzhou. He had opened a tailor shop at No. 5 Songbai Lane, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei. A few days ago, he returned to his village for some business and met a relative, Li Fengshan, who told him that his two sons, Li Qiaogen and Li Qiaosheng, were suddenly kidnapped by bandits in Linjia Lane, Yangcheng River on the tenth of last month. Later, he sent a letter demanding a ransom, with half a card as proof of the ransom negotiation, and asked someone to go to Room 12, Pingqiao Hotel, Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai to negotiate. Because my family lives in Shanghai, Li gave me the card and asked me to inquire at any time whether there was such a person as Li Jinshan. After I finished my business and returned to Shanghai, I went to Room 12 of the Pingqiao Hotel this morning to ask about Li Jinshan. According to the tea attendant, Li is now at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Tibet Road, so I went to that place and saw Wang and suspected that he was Li Jinshan, so I stepped forward to ask, etc. The head of the detective office verified the confession and found that Tian's words were hesitant and suspicious, so he ordered him to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the detective office, rose to state the case, saying that the detective office had not yet investigated the truth of the case, and whether Tian's confession was true, so he did not prosecute him and requested permission to detain him for investigation. He then submitted the half card as evidence. According to the previous complaint of Wang, the detective, Tian Xinsong confessed as above. Judge Wu Tingqi ordered Tian to be detained until the 30th of this month for further questioning.

Jin Shunxing Fishing Boat Sunk in Collision 181

▲ Eight Fishermen Killed

▲ Yu Shun Has Left Shanghai

▲ This Matter Still Needs Investigation

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Yu Shun" steamer came to Shanghai from Xiamen on the 12th of this month to unload cargo and passengers and was then sent to Yantai to load Liu Zhennian's troops and head to Wenzhou, Zhejiang. The steamer arrived in Shanghai just as the new and old managers of the company were changing over and did not stay long before leaving the port. The steamer was returning to Shanghai from Xiamen when, at 3:00 PM on the 11th, it was near the Putuo sea area when a "Jin Shunxing" fishing boat loaded with fresh fish was returning to Shenjiamen. The "Yu Shun" steamer was also traveling from south to north when it approached the fishing boat but did not sound its whistle. The "Jin Shunxing" boat failed to avoid it and was hit in the middle. The fishing boat was cut in two and immediately sank. The "Yu Shun" steamer immediately turned back to help rescue. There were four small sampans and fishermen Liu Guoquan, Lin Aman, Liu Anbang, Liu Ashi, Wu Yangmu, Wu Yangdan, Huang Tonghui, Wang Zhongsheng, and others, eight in total, who fell into the sea and drowned. The remaining 19 crew members were rescued by civilian ships (4 people), while the remaining 15 people climbed onto the "Yu Shun." The "Yu Shun" steamer's passengers saw these shipwrecked crew members and scrambled to donate money, raising more than 90 yuan. On the 12th, when the ship arrived in Shanghai, the "Yu Shun" steamer crew sent the 15 rescued people to the Quanzhang Association in Longhua Road, where Mr. Guo in the association took them in. The "Jin Shunxing" was a newly built fishing boat. A telegram has been sent to the boat owner asking them to come to Shanghai to negotiate with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The bereaved family of the 8 deceased has requested compensation. The fellow villagers are requested to provide assistance. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has not yet received a detailed report from the "Yu Shun" steamer on this matter and has not yet expressed an opinion.

Taxpayers' Association Requests Restoration of Water Prices 182

▲ Letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council

The Taxpaying Chinese Residents' Association yesterday received a letter from the Dinghai Fellow Association forwarding a letter to the Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council, saying that the Dinghai residents in Shanghai wrote that there are fellow villagers living in single-family houses at Nos. 2530 and 2531 Zhoujiazui Road. The rent for each house is 18 yuan per month, and there are five houses in total, with two houses occupied by laundry businesses. Before the installation of water meters, the water fee was 1 yuan and 25 cents per month for each house. After the installation of water meters, the water fee for the five houses was 76 yuan in just 28 days. The water fee has always been borne by the landlord. Now the landlord wants the tenants to install water meters themselves, but the tenants are mostly laborers and cannot afford to install them. Yesterday morning, the water company closed the water supply, causing the tenants to suddenly have no water and unable to live in peace. They requested that a solution be found to provide relief. Therefore, please forward the request for negotiation for the public good. It is noted that the water fee problem has been solved by the Council convening representatives from the water company, real estate association, and other parties to negotiate a win-win solution. Now the water company wants to solve the problem by cutting off the water, which may only increase the seriousness of the security problem and cause anxiety for the Director-General and the Association. Furthermore, the purpose of installing water meters to calculate water fees is to control waste, not to increase the water company's revenue, which is something that the Director-General attaches special importance to. Now, the water company has not achieved the purpose of controlling waste, and the so-called discount method has changed from 7.5% to an increase of one-third, which is about 10%. Isn't the installation of water meters for the purpose of increasing prices? In view of the above reasons, please ask the Council to quickly order the water company to restore the water supply to maintain the lives of the people. This letter is addressed to the Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council.

Russian Fishing Boat Owner Reports Experience of Escaping Danger 183

According to the Shanghai Times, the owner of the Russian fishing boat "Sakto," which arrived in Shanghai from Vladivostok on Sunday, reported to the Commercial Affairs Office of the China Eastern Railway in Shanghai that five teenagers mutinied on the boat 60 miles after it left Vladivostok, imprisoning him for two days without water or food. Later, during a storm, they forced him to hand over his pistol and ordered him to drive the boat. After safely navigating two major dangers, when they arrived in Shanghai, Mr. Ke took the opportunity to leave the boat and wandered blindly for two days before finding the China Eastern Railway Office to report everything. Coincidentally, Patrol Chief Wu Feide of the Water Police Station boarded the boat to inquire. A teenager admitted that the boat owner had shown a certificate, but his behavior was suspicious. After being notified by the China Eastern Railway Office, the boat was returned to the China Eastern Railway Office and the five teenagers were ordered to disembark. The boat is now guarded by the original boat owner, Mr. Ke, and a crew member, and efforts will be made to send it back to Vladivostok.

Husband and Wife Both Jump into River, Neither Dies 186

▲ Silent After Meeting

▲ Water Police Provide Guidance

Ye Yinbao, 21 years old, from Sanbei, is a cigarette paper shopkeeper. He married a fellow villager, Tong Xinghua (18 years old), in April of this year. Ye lost his job due to the Shanghai war and planned to move his small family to his father Ye Shengzhang's home at No. 39 Anping Street in the city. However, Xinghua did not want to live with her in-laws and preferred to live alone with her sister in Xiangyanqiao, so the couple was often at odds. They once went to court but still reconciled. Yesterday, Ye went to Xiangyanqiao again to call his wife home. The two walked to the Waibaidu Bridge, but Xinghua said that she was tired and could not walk and asked to take a tram. Ye refused because he had no money with him. The two started arguing again. Ye became extremely angry and stood on the bridge, suddenly jumping into the Suzhou Creek to commit suicide. Xinghua was shocked and went to the Xinguang Wharf alone. Because her husband was dead, she had no face to go home and also jumped into the river to commit suicide. Fortunately, she was rescued by others and sent to the Central Police Station. However, Ye was rescued by the night watchman No. 6 shortly after entering the water and sent to the Customs Water Police Station. After changing his dry clothes, the Central Police Station telegraphed to inform them that Xinghua had been rescued after jumping into the river. The police station immediately sent someone to bring Xinghua back. The couple met silently at the Water Police Station. The police officers persuaded them and ordered detective Shen Changshan to summon Ye's father, Ye Shengzhang, to the case and take the two of them back.

Fictitious Money Shop Cheats Deposits 187

Xing Shenzhi, from Jiangyin, recently colluded with Gu Bingyao and Qian Yangsheng to lease the premises at No. 28 Ruyili, Henan Road, and set up a fictitious Hongxing Money Shop. Xing acted as the street runner, while Gu and Qian served as the managers and deputy managers, touting for deposits all day long, boasting about how sufficient their capital was. Those who did not know the inside story came to them in droves, depositing cash into the shop, collecting checkbooks, and issuing checks. When the check holders went to them to cash the checks, Xing and the others had already defrauded a large sum of money and divided it up and escaped. The affected shops reported to the chief patrol station in charge and requested an investigation. It was not until around 1:00 AM yesterday that detective Gao Zhen discovered that Xing Shenzhi was hiding in Room 372 of the Dajiangnan Hotel on Fujian Road and immediately rushed to arrest him. Under questioning at the police station, he confessed that Gu Bingyao lived at No. 13 Tianbaoli, Xinjiang Road, Zhabei, and that he did not know Qian Yangsheng's whereabouts. When detective Gao went to Gu's home, Gu had already absconded after hearing the news. At 9:00 AM, Xing Shenzhi was sent to the First Special District Local Court. Judge Liu Yugui summoned him for questioning. The police station lawyer Qian Xunjiu said that the defendant had colluded with others to set up a fictitious money shop to defraud deposits. It has now been found that the Dunyu Cloth Shop at No. 188 Jiujiang Road had deposited 1,008 taels of silver, the Gengyu Silk Shop at No. 710 Jiu'anli, Fujian Road had deposited 800 taels of silver, the Defengchang at No. 70 Hongyufang, Zhengjia Wood Bridge had deposited 500 yuan in foreign currency, and the Lixing Foreign Firm at No. 2 Beijing Road had deposited 550 taels of silver. The Qinfeng Yarn Factory at No. 161 Rue Labrousse in the French Concession had deposited 619 taels of silver. In addition, there may be other victims who still need to be investigated. He requested a postponement of the hearing and a continued investigation. Staff members from Dunyu and other shops were sent to the court to state the circumstances of the fraud. Judge Liu then questioned the defendant and ordered him to be detained and the hearing postponed for further investigation.

Yang Xixian Debt Case Criminal Prosecution Unfounded 188

Yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m., the Fifth Tribunal of the Special First District heard the case of Yang Xixian's debt dispute with Zhang Tinggui. The judge first asked Yang Xixian when he bought the American cotton from Meian Foreign Firm. Yang replied that he did not buy the American cotton from Meian, but from Zhang Tinggui personally. He had bought it several times, the last time being 100 bales, worth over 14,000 taels. At that time, three checks were issued, two expiring on October 18, and the date of the remaining one forgotten. Yang also stated that after buying the yarn factory from the Japanese in 1931, he added yarn spindles. Unexpectedly, the market has been sluggish recently, and the January 28th Incident last year further exacerbated the situation. Finally, the funds could not be turned over, leading to a mid-way setback. There was no intention to defraud and take property. Zhang Tinggui then appeared in court. The judge asked whether the American cotton was sold by Meian Foreign Firm. Zhang replied that it was sold personally, but the goods came from Meian. The judge further asked how the over 14,000 taels of debt would be handled. Yang replied that he was trying his best to find a way. The judge further asked why the bank did not honor the checks he issued. Yang replied that the bank heard that the factory's finances were very tight, so it returned them. Lawyer Li Zuyu, representing Yang, stood up and stated that Longmao was a limited company, and Yang was the manager. All the funds involved were advanced by the company, and the orders were placed by the company, not for personal business. Therefore, the criminal charge should not stand. The police lawyer stated that after the defendant bought the American cotton, he mortgaged it to the bank and transferred the funds for other uses. Therefore, the police believed that there was a crime of defrauding and taking property. Lawyer Li stated that the checks issued at ordinary times were honored by the bank. This time, the return of the checks was unexpected. Moreover, all the American cotton received was in the factory warehouse and had not been mortgaged to the bank. The judge asked Yang whether the factory was operating as usual when he bought the American cotton. Yang replied that the factory only announced its liquidation on November 6. The judge further asked whether there was any transaction with Zhongnan a few days before October 18. Yang replied that there was, and asked to check the account books. Lawyer Li then presented the account books. The judge asked whether the 100 bales of American cotton were mortgaged to Zhongnan. Yang replied that they were still in the factory's third warehouse for spinning. The judge said to the plaintiff that the defendant admitted to owing you money, but the check was returned due to credit issues. Lawyer Li stood up and said that the plaintiff did not understand the true situation beforehand, and heard that the factory owed a huge amount of money, so there seemed to be a suspicion of fraud. Now that the general situation is clear, could the court dismiss the criminal part? The police lawyer said that according to the report of the plaintiff Zhang Tinggui, the defendant mortgaged the goods to Zhongnan in October, and announced the liquidation in November. Therefore, the police believed that the defendant was suspected of fraud. Now that the lawsuit is in progress, the plaintiff and defendant can reconcile outside the court, so the private prosecution can be withdrawn, but the public prosecution cannot be withdrawn immediately. Lawyer Li stated that the factory's dealings with Zhongnan used up to 130,000 taels at most, and the last time the check was returned, only 22,000 taels were overdrawn. Therefore, the return of the check was unexpected by the defendant. If the police believe that the non-payment of the check is fraud, then all ordinary loans that are repaid with checks but not honored will be considered fraud, which seems to be too excessive in law. Finally, the judge announced that Yang Xixian was innocent of the criminal charge. If the police have any objections, they can file another lawsuit in the civil court, and then declared the court adjourned.

Recent News from the China Life Insurance Advancement Society 195

According to a report from the China Life Insurance Advancement Society on the life insurance business in the United States, according to the reports of various life insurance companies in the United States, in 1931, among the compensation paid due to the death of the insured, there were US$60.2 million, equivalent to 30 million yuan in Chinese currency. The insured (commonly known as policyholders) were about 97,800 people who died within one year of purchasing life insurance. Among them, 25,000 people died within three months of purchasing insurance, and more than 1,000 people died within one week of purchasing insurance. Several hundred people died after the insurance medical examination before receiving the insurance policy. However, because the insurance premium was paid in full when the application was signed on the spot to the life insurance company, the insurance policy took effect immediately. Even if the insurance policy has not been issued, the family can receive compensation. From this, we can know the impermanence of human life.

Judge Feithang's Report on the Shanghai International Settlement, Volume 4 (26) 201

11 Being in a state of economic distress caused by recklessness or other inexcusable reasons and prejudicial to the proper discharge of his duties; or

12 Divulging information obtained in the performance of public duties, otherwise than in the performance of public duties, or, even without divulging such information, using information obtained as a civil servant or communicated by others for purposes other than the performance of public duties; or

13 Accepting or soliciting any commission, fee or reward, whether in money or otherwise, for the performance of duties without the approval of the committee (the salary due for the performance of duties is not included), or failing to report to the head of his office when asked for any such commission, fee or reward, or failing to report to the head of his department if he is the head of the office, or failing to report to the chief of the department if he is the head of the department; or

14 Misusing or improperly using any government property under circumstances not sufficient to constitute a criminal case; or

15 Committing a criminal offense; or

16 Leaving his post without leave or without legitimate reason; or

17 Knowingly making a statement that is inaccurate or false, but making an inaccurate or false statement to obtain his public position or rights or benefits of employment, or to prejudice public service or the government.

Pension (Sections 26, 31, 34 to 39 and 42)

The pension is based on the amount of donations paid (the pension for defense forces and police officers is provided for separately, and the provisions summarized below relate to the pension for other staff).

With very limited exceptions, every civil servant must, from the date of his appointment, contribute 4% of the salary from which he is eligible to receive a pension to the pension fund. The amount of this contribution is deducted from the official's monthly salary, and the Federal Revenue Administration Fund periodically allocates an amount equal to the total amount contributed by each civil servant to the pension fund.

The annual pension to which a civil servant is entitled upon retirement is based on the average salary from which the civil servant is eligible to receive a pension during the entire period of donation to the pension fund or during the last 25 years. Of these two periods, the shorter one shall be used and shall be calculated at one-sixtieth of the average salary from which the pension can be drawn for each year of donation to the pension fund, but no person shall receive any pension unless he has donated to the pension fund for ten years or more.

A civil servant has the right to retire at the age of sixty, and unless he is recommended by the committee to remain in office until the age of sixty-five without retiring, a civil servant must retire when he reaches the age of sixty.

The retirement age for female civil servants is stipulated earlier.

A civil servant has no right to retire with a pension at the age of fifty-five, but may be allowed to retire with a pension.

A civil servant who has donated to the pension fund for ten years or more and is not yet fifty-five years old and is dismissed for the legitimate reasons mentioned above for not reaching the retirement age, but is not dismissed because of the official's own misconduct, may receive the above-mentioned part of the pension calculated in proportion to the years of service.

A civil servant who retires for any of these reasons after donating to the pension fund for less than ten years, and a female civil servant who is dismissed due to marriage, may receive from the pension fund twice the amount contributed by each of them, but without interest.

A civil servant who voluntarily retires before reaching old age due to reasons other than illness due to his own fault may receive back the amount he has contributed without interest if he has donated to the pension fund for less than fifteen years. If he has donated to the pension fund for more than fifteen years, he may receive a pension calculated in proportion to the number of years he has donated, the longer the number of years of donation, the more he will receive.

A civil servant who is dismissed for misconduct or voluntarily retires or is ordered to resign to avoid dismissal shall only receive back the amount he has contributed without interest.

A civil servant who is injured in the performance of his duties, not due to his own fault, but specifically due to the performance of his duties, so that he has to retire before reaching old age, has special provisions for the amount of pension he should receive each year. (End)

Free Talk

Symphony of Peace and War 202

— Rong Yu

│Contradiction and Ridicule│

The kind and amiable old pastor is preaching about "universal love" and going to "heaven"; the men and women in the seats are singing hymns and making sincere prayers. This church is truly filled with an atmosphere of peace and kindness, and pleasant and sweet singing. Where is heaven? Heaven is here! Where is the God of peace? The God of peace is also here! So on Sundays when I have nothing to do, I often come to this hall to sit, seeking temporary comfort in my soul, and witnessing the appearance of the God of peace for a moment. However, this church is only three miles away from the park's target range. Every time there is a pious service, it is also the time when the Japanese army is training diligently. The sound of Gedeng's machine guns and the crackling of rifles always break the air in the hall. Inside the hall is a burst of singing and prayer, and outside the hall is a burst of gunfire, as if a symphony is being played. However, this song seems too ridiculous and contradictory! Comparing the two sides, one is a kind smile and the other is a ferocious murderous aura; one side is persuading you to return to heaven, and the other is sending you to the land of death; this side is a world of peace, harmony, joy, kindness, and the other side is a realm of terror, cruelty, death, and annihilation. Moreover, further speaking, the peace in the hall is genuinely outward, but who can say that the old pastor or the men and women will not reveal their ferocious faces and cruel means once they leave the church? This shows that the realization of peace is very difficult. And the Japanese army's guns and cannons, although they are drills and exercises, like the tricks of January 28th, there is always the possibility of a real performance, which shows that the danger of war is imminent.

Alas! Peace, war, this symphony is played everywhere and at all times at home, abroad, and all over the world. Don't you see the great powers desperately expanding their armaments? But at the disarmament conference, you also propose to limit airplanes and cannons; I also propose to save military spending. Isn't Japan, our eastern neighbor, always shouting about Sino-Japanese friendship and co-existence and co-prosperity? But he swallowed the fat meat of the Northeast in one gulp: Shanghai's Zhabei was also messed up by his airplanes and cannons. In addition, there are many such phenomena. Peace and war are symphonizing, it's really ridiculous! It's really contradictory!

Flattery 203

— Yan Chonglou

│Is Sinful│

I talked about the sin of "cursing" in this journal a few days ago, and now I will talk about the sin of "flattery."

Except for Zilu, it can be said that no one is not "angry when they hear criticism and happy when they hear praise." Originally, if a person has a fault, then they have a fault, and if a person has praise, then they have praise. However, there is a kind of person in society who specializes in catering to the psychology of the world. If you have no praise, he will praise you, and even if you have a fault, he will praise you. This is the so-called art of flattery.

People who are good at flattery and ingratiating themselves can use various flattering techniques to flatter you in order to achieve their purpose of flattering you. On the side being flattered, because flattery makes people lose their minds, they will unknowingly fall into the art of flattery!

"People who flatter others have lost their nobility!" People who flatter others, although they have lost their noble personality, they can use the results of their flattery to act like bullies! Based on the above discussion, we can get a new discovery, which is! "The more a person exaggerates in front of others, the more servile he is."

Flattery is sinful, flattery is harmful, and if you want to prevent flattery, you must be able to fulfill the two principles of "fearing when you hear praise! rejoicing when you hear criticism!"

The Difficulty of Renting a House in the World 204

— Jin Butong

│The Difficulty of Eating Comes Second│

"There is nothing more difficult than eating in the world." Although the problem of eating is the most difficult in the world, there are now economists and sociologists who are loaded with truckloads, wearing three thousand-degree nearsighted glasses, shaking their heads and studying, and generally in the near future,

Perhaps they can come up with a way for everyone to have food to eat, to solve the difficulty. So I think the most difficult thing in the world in the future will definitely not be eating, but renting a house.

I was originally an only child who came to Shanghai to make a living. But when I first arrived in Shanghai, it was really difficult to find a place to shelter from the wind and rain. When I saw the red rental sign and knocked on the door, eleven out of ten houses refused to rent to those without family. Later, I still relied on the kindness of an old uncle, who took on one hundred and twenty points of responsibility, to rent a small room just enough to accommodate my stinky body as a mansion at night.

It was terrible. Once it came to summer, the stuffiness and heat were still secondary, because I had been injected with a preventive vaccine and was not afraid of getting a fever, but thousands of bedbugs completely relied on me to provide food, and I couldn't bear some of the burden. So I decided to move to a better place. Suffer once, learn once, this time I decided to bring my wife and two children from the countryside to live with me, relying on the signboard to avoid bumping into the nails of those who refuse to rent to those without family.

I brought my wife and sons, saw the red rental sign, and knocked on the door. The landlady of the second landlord opened her mouth and asked how many people there were. I said two couples, two children, and a maid. The landlady of the second landlord said that there were no children in this house, and it was too troublesome to have children, so she wouldn't rent. I bumped into another nail, so when I saw the red rental sign, I first stuck my ears to the crack in the door to listen. Later, I heard the sound of children crying inside, so I hurriedly knocked on the door. The landlady of the second landlord shook her head incessantly when she saw me, and said repeatedly, "I won't rent, I won't rent. My own children are already making a terrible noise. If I bring two more, the house will collapse."

Napoleon said: There are no difficult words in the dictionary. If he comes to Shanghai, he will definitely say, "Renting a house is difficult."

Fork in the Road of Death (108) 205

— Fan Yanqiao

However, after experiencing more, Guang Ye became more powerful, and in addition to art, there were some conditions to consider. So among the twenty-odd dancing girls in the Neon Dance Hall, only one caught Mu Liang's eye, and this person was called Jiang Aili.

After eleven o'clock, more and more dancers came, and the band played even more powerfully. Pairs of dancers were colorful and mixed, which really fit the poem: "Falling flowers and butterflies fly in groups." Aili is a star in the Neon Dance Hall, and naturally very busy. It is not easy for Mu Liang to catch her. Mu Liang had to use champagne to curry favor with her, one bottle, two bottles, and in tense times, it was not certain that he would open half a dozen a night. Later, he understood the trick, so he simply went later, and he would never go back until the music stopped, the lights went out, and the dancing girls put on their capes and coats, ready to walk out of the dance hall. This was the opportunity to have a short secret word with Aili, but Aili was very playful, and no matter what, she always said:

"I'm sorry, I have a bad headache, I have to go to sleep, see you tomorrow." Before he could say anything more, she flew a kiss to him, and got into the pre-hired white-brand car and drove away.

When Mu Liang returned to the rented mansion in a trance, his wife was always fast asleep. It was not until the next day, when the sun was high, that Mu Liang got up and asked him, "What time did you come back last night? Where were you playing again?" Mu Liang stammered and made up a lie at will, and it passed.

One day, Mu Liang came back extraordinarily early, and his wife was also surprised, and said, "You don't have an appointment tonight."

Mu Liang said listlessly, "Um"!

Han Dashao Nai said, "Today's radio report said that the 19th Route Army retreated to the second line of defense, and Suzhou is going to be tight." Mu Liang only answered "Um" again. He felt that he was too unconcerned about national affairs, and reluctantly said again, "Really?" Han Dashao Nai said, "How can it not be true! I just heard the "Shen Bao Extra" being sold outside the door, and it also said the same, but there is also good news, we are about to make peace."

The last sentence was enough to cheer up Mu Liang and say:

"Anyway, we can't beat them, it's better to make peace as soon as possible, otherwise we will be shouting for long-term resistance in Luoyang. The essence of the southeast is about to end." It was rare that he was happy today. Since he fled to Shanghai to avoid the war, the criticism of national affairs has decreased day by day, or the air in the concession has a kind of incredible magic that makes people numb and decadent.

Han Dashao Nai was also excited a lot. She put down the velvet rope vest and needles in her hand, walked closer to him, sat down, and prepared to have a long conversation with him. Said:

"Thank God, let's end it soon. Living in this spiral shell is extremely boring. Walking six feet away has become our Jiangbei shed outside Suzhou City."

— Song and Music by Gao Tianqi

My China, has vast land and abundant resources, why is it poor and weak, national shame has accumulated, foreign troubles are pressing, economic aggression is the most fierce, compatriots have never realized, still drowsy in a dream! But such as drawing enjoyment, Li Mi's habits become the wind, domestic goods are rejected, foreign goods are praised, don't let us shout slogans, implement ourselves, ask for hygiene, simple is better than rich; carved source is exhausted and overflows, the national capital is naturally empty, want to seek to save the country want to seek lightweight and warm, cloth clothes are better than wool, a thatched house in Fengfa, to save the country first save the poor, the only good way to save the poor, two, is also comfortable and rich, Hua Wu Xian Yi Dian food, non-frugality does not work! Develop a delicate mood and become a weak worm! You don't see, the great Yu who worked hard and endured hardship, ate poorly and lived cheaply; you don't see, the hero who slept on firewood and tasted gall and avenged his shame and revived the country.

Speech

The Type of Person I Fear Most 207

— Buddha

The other day, while visiting a large-scale exhibition, I ran into an old friend I hadn't seen in years. During our idle chat, he suddenly asked me directly, "What type of person do you fear the most?" I replied, "There are very few people I fear, but there is one type I fear the most."

He then asked, "What type of person is that? Surely not a robber?" I said, "No, I have no wealth. Why would I fear them?" He guessed again, "A kidnapper?" I said, "Even less likely. I don't have the qualifications for that." He continued, "Could it be those heroic figures who rob on the road and slaughter pigs?" I laughed, "The shabby clothes I wear and the fact that my purse is often 'bust' – what's there to fear?" He then guessed, "Perhaps you fear officials the most?" I said, "I never do anything illegal in my life, so why should I fear officials?"

My friend then laughed and said, "So, what kind of person do you fear?" I said, "I fear those thick-skinned fellows the most. As the saying goes, 'Nothing is difficult in the world, except for a thick face.' I fear those with thick faces the most. Suppose I criticize them for their lack of virtue and chastity, they readily reply, 'She's already been with every man, and I make a living from it.' Suppose I point out their thieving behavior, they unhesitatingly reply, 'I've been committing crimes all my life; it's just my old habit.' If I encounter people like this, I get a headache and have no way to deal with them."

Originally, in a society, a good society, the reason it can maintain its virtuous state is nothing other than morality, the so-called "a sense of shame and a sense of right and wrong, everyone has it". But thick-skinned people completely shatter a sense of shame and a sense of right and wrong. The little magic lantern of society is torn apart by them. How can we reason with them?

My friend nodded in agreement and then we parted ways at the exhibition.

Literary Arts

Evening View from an Autumn Suburb 209

— Wu Daohua

Slowly walking through desolate suburbs, lost in thought, I wander alone. The setting sun casts a dim light on the river village. Fallen leaves from the woods descend like rain. Cold waves roll in from the docking area. Wisps of smoke entwine with the returning geese. Scattered fishing lights mirror the sleeping gulls. Alas, everything is a scene of autumn. My eyes strain towards the distant sky, filled with endless melancholy.

Written on My Pillow on a Cold Night - Chen Bao Ren 210

Unable to sleep on a cold night, the lamp flickers dimly. The quilt feels cold, and I sense the heavy frost. In the stillness, I hear the sound of falling leaves. I sigh at the many sorrows of the world. I regret that my studies have yet to bring me fame. As the neighbor's rooster crows, signaling the dawn, I lean on my pillow, my melancholy unresolved.

Science

Essential Requirements for Dyes 211

— Zuo Qi

The quality of dyes is generally judged by whether they fade or not. However, there are two different viewpoints on what is meant by "not fading." From the perspective of ordinary buyers, "not fading" refers to being resistant to light and washing. From the perspective of dyers and textile manufacturers, "not fading" has a much broader meaning. In addition to the two conditions mentioned above, dyes must also be able to withstand the various procedures involved in weaving. The essential requirements for dyes are described in detail below.

(1) Light Resistance: This is the most important point. If the color gradually loses its intensity and luster under the action of sunlight, it is said to fade; otherwise, it is said to be non-fading. However, among all the colors known today, none can absolutely withstand prolonged exposure to sunlight. All colors will fade to some extent, only at different speeds. Therefore, "non-fading" is a relative term.

The German scholar Gustave Schultz has divided dyes into several categories according to their light resistance. Those that can withstand sunlight for up to 30 days without fading are classified as first-class. Those that fade within three days or completely lose their color by the end of 28 days are classified as the lowest class.

(2) Wash Resistance: This refers to the ability to resist the action of boiling water or cold water and soap. Regarding this point, Schultz divides dyes into five categories, with those that do not fade in boiling water being classified as first-class and those that fade in cold water being classified as the lowest class. However, there are cases where the dye itself does not fade but bleeds into nearby white materials. Therefore, when distinguishing whether a fabric is wash-resistant, we must pay attention to two points: first, whether the water becomes discolored; second, whether the dye bleeds into nearby pure white materials.

(3) Rub Resistance: The color does not transfer to a white cloth when rubbed against it.

(4) Steam Resistance: The dye on the fabric must not show any signs of weakening under the action of steam.

(5) Iron Resistance: The dye on the fabric must be able to withstand the heat of the iron without peeling off.

(6) Smoke Resistance: Fabrics that need to be bleached after dyeing, such as felt carpets, are often smoked with sulfur. Therefore, the dye used must be able to resist the action of sulfur without changing.

Dyes are classified into acid dyes, basic dyes, sulfide dyes, direct dyes, mordant dyes, etc. Since their properties are different, their resistance or fastness to various actions also varies. Among them, the color dyed with mordant dyes is the most fast and does not change easily when exposed to sunlight, water washing, alkalis, friction, or hot irons. It is a pity that the dyeing method is more complicated.

News Digest

Dispute over a Will 212

— Kang Shi

▲ Importance of Punctuation

This story is not something I fabricated. I saw it in a Chinese textbook. It is very interesting and has some literary merit, so it can be used as a topic of conversation after dinner. I have no intention of plagiarizing or picking up leftovers.

There was a wealthy man named Zhang who was old and had no sons, only a daughter. He married a man into his family. Many years later, Zhang's concubine gave birth to a son, named Yifei. So the family all called him A-Yi.

When Yifei was four years old, Zhang became very ill. According to Chinese customs, the son-in-law has the right to inherit the property. So,

Page 23

the concubine was deeply worried that the son-in-law would seize the property, and even cried! So she approached Zhang. Zhang then wrote a will for her and said, "But you must be patient for a long time before you can be free from worry!" At the same time, he summoned his son-in-law and falsely said, "A-Yi is young and unreliable. All my property is given to you, but you must support him and his mother!" He also took out a will for him, and read:

Zhang Yifei not my son family property all give to my son-in-law outsiders may not contest

After Zhang died, the son-in-law took possession of the entire inheritance and treated Yifei as a servant. Of course, excessive oppression will inevitably lead to stronger resistance. So Yifei, under oppression, went to the authorities to seek justice and filed a lawsuit to recover the property. The son-in-law presented Zhang's will to the official, who read it and found that it was the same as the will presented by Yifei, except that the son-in-law's will had no punctuation. So he said to Zhang's son-in-law, "Your father-in-law, because Yifei was young, was afraid that he would seize the property and be harmed by you. So he deliberately made the will seem as if Yifei was not his son, and he did not use punctuation, clearly deceiving you to manage these properties for a few years!" He then took out Yifei's will and read:

Zhang Yifei, my son also, family property all give; my son-in-law, outsider, may not contest

The official then ruled that Zhang's property should all belong to Yifei. The above story is to show the disadvantages of not using punctuation. So it seems that the modern advocacy of new-style punctuation has this meaning!

Random Ramblings

The Autobiography of a Rickshaw Puller 213

— Kuang Wenbing

Next door to my stall selling bedsheets is a small hotel, located in a desolate area of Zhabei. Although that's how it is, there are still many coolies, rickshaw pullers, and short-trousered friends hauling mud who come and go. The hotel relies entirely on them. They are truly the world's heavy drinkers. Eating seems secondary. A catty of white liquor, two shots of unrefined wine, that's what each of them can drink down. When they get drunk, their faces turn red, and veins appear on their legs. That's when they're at their strongest. So they sing loudly, so they forget the hypocrisy, coldness, cruelty, and the various pains of life. One day, I was reading Bai Juyi's "The Charcoal Seller" until the line "Pitifully, the clothes on his body are thin, he worries about the low price of charcoal and wishes for colder weather," stroking the scroll and reciting at length, when their yelling completely startled me out of my thoughts. So I stepped out the door and saw a rickshaw puller sitting cross-legged at a square table at the hotel entrance, his drunken state hazy, almost triumphant. I unintentionally asked:

"Why are you so happy?" This touched his heartstrings, and he told me in a torrent of words:

"In this day and age, business is really not working out. Thirty-six trades, none of them are profitable. Eleven years ago, I was a carpenter in × village in Haimen. I earned two jiao a day, and I struggled to live frugally for three years, accumulating one hundred yuan, and married a good wife. Who knew that my fate would get even worse from then on? Just ten months later, she gave birth to a small child. One was not enough; the next day, her stomach suddenly cramped, and she gave birth to another one. That was terrible! At that time, business in the town was also slow. There weren't even two days of work in three days, and we were often hungry. Later, a few good friends pooled together two hundred yuan and started a carpentry shop ourselves. The workers were lazy and sloppy, and in less than half a year, the shop was forced to close. It was really worrying. I don't know why, but I suddenly thought of coming to Shanghai to pull a rickshaw.

Life in hardship, passing the days like years, pulling a rickshaw is not a life after all!

Fortunately, I have a naturally strong frame. My arms were trained with an axe (stretching out his right hand forcefully), so pulling a rickshaw doesn't feel too tiring. It's just these two legs (patting his legs) that can't take it. At first, after pulling for three days,

my legs ached to the bone, and even my back was sore. Lying on the bed, I couldn't catch my breath for a long time, and I couldn't stretch my legs straight, and bending them was even more painful. I lay in bed for a full week before gradually recovering. So I went back to pulling, and I've been pulling until now. My bones are all stiff! Alas! I've simply lost all feeling. Eleven years, ah!

Speaking of the income from pulling a rickshaw, it's really getting worse every year. The number of pullers is only increasing, but the licenses are limited! It can't exceed ten thousand. Renting a shift car costs one thousand yuan. Renting in the concession is even more unbearable! One dollar and forty cents, from six o'clock in the morning to ten o'clock at night, is considered handing over a day's fate. After returning the car to the company, there are less than a few dozen copper coins left. I put them in my wife's hand, and she just smiles bitterly for a while.

If you want business to be good, you only need a sudden burst of wind and rain. Last year, on August 27th, there was that big storm. The floodwater in the street reached my knees, but I was stuck at home with diarrhea, watching people earn money quickly with dry eyes. A'nian next door earned nine dollars that day. It was a great opportunity, but I missed it! (Pounding his chest with his hand). Pulling a rickshaw, it's not good to eat too much. If you eat too much, not only can you not pull, but also your stomach will hurt. The people sitting in the car don't care, they always kick and scold. In eleven years, I have rarely eaten a full meal on time. I always buy a sesame cake to eat here, or eat a bowl of porridge there, or drink half a catty of old white wine, or take two shots of unrefined wine. A family of four, two small children, myself and my wife. Fortunately, she didn't give birth to a third one! The monthly rent is one and a half dollars, for a dark and gloomy loft. Four hundred and fifty cash for rice a day. This year is good, the price of rice is cheap, and we can still buy white rice with four hundred and fifty cash. Two jiao for vegetables and tofu, plus wine and cigarettes, it costs at least fifteen dollars a month to make ends meet. Fortunately, my wife sells water caltrops every day and can earn a few hundred cash to make up for the shortfall. Otherwise, I'd really be too poor to make ends meet.

In this day and age, business is really not working out. Pulling a rickshaw is not a life. But what can I do!

At this time, his drunken state seemed to have subsided. I also, driven by the demands of life, said goodbye to him and returned to my own room to write.

School Life

The Art of Eating 214

— Zhao Jun

Speaking of student life, it is indeed meaningful, especially the issue of eating. Usually, you can be late or leave early for class, and some wealthy students treat the school as a hotel, but as soon as the dinner bell rings, they scramble to be the first, afraid of being left behind. That kind of spirit, except for watching a ball game, is not easily seen. If you are one step behind, those who arrive first have already issued a mobilization order, devouring food like wolves, each showing their skills, and you can only sigh at the empty bowl. The spirit of humility is absolutely impossible to find in the dining hall. Therefore, for the sake of eating, strange and bizarre tricks are played out in society every day.

I boarded at school, and for the sake of eating, I don't know how many losses I suffered. Therefore, I had to study countermeasures on how to deal with this kind of environment. Now, I dare not keep my research secret, and I am publishing it for everyone to see.

The art of eating, in other words, is the art of eating vegetables. There is a lot of rice and little vegetables. According to the law of supply and demand in economics, the demand for vegetables naturally exceeds the supply. The policy is the "accuracy, patience, ruthlessness" three-character doctrine.

First, let's talk about accuracy. When eating, you should arrive on time, never be late, the so-called "past due is not waiting," sitting and missing the opportunity. The first thing to do when you sit down is to see clearly which dishes are good and what the ingredients are. For example, for meat, see clearly which piece is moderately lean and fat, of good quality, and large in quantity. Never focus on quantity and forget quality, or you will choose a bone and then be greatly disappointed. Therefore, you must be prepared before picking up your chopsticks, so as not to have nothing to aim for and be outdone by those who are quick-eyed and fast-handed. There is also a relationship between the order in which you eat dishes. You should eat the larger pieces first, such as fish, meat, and meatballs, because there are not many of these. But for things like stir-fried shredded pork, no one will carefully pick out the shredded pork to eat, so it doesn't matter if you're a bit slower.

Let's talk about patience again. When the dish is in hand, sometimes the dish is too hot. You should be patient no matter what. If you can't be patient, people will send one piece after another to their mouths, and there will be very few dishes in the bowl. Wouldn't you lose out? Sometimes you take advantage and enjoy more delicious food. People can't help but show displeasure, or mock you a few times. You can just turn a deaf ear and remain patient. Speaking of ruthlessness, in addition to accuracy and patience, you must also be ruthless. One piece after another, one spoonful after another, be as ruthless as possible, otherwise the things in the plate will be swept away. Haven't you heard that "nothing is difficult in the world, only fearing a thick face"? If your face isn't thick and your heart isn't ruthless, you can forget about getting a good deal. I think this accuracy, patience, and ruthlessness three-character doctrine will be of some help when eating.

Short Story

The Narrow Definition of Law 215

— Yu Cheng

The main room in a certain county bureau in the morning was filled with smoke, as if there was a fire. The electric light was dyed a dim yellow. A couple was lying on the exquisite brass bed, puffing out clouds of smoke, thus bathing the entire room in the atmosphere.

They smoked wildly for a long time, as if their spirits were aroused. Then they opened the talk box. The man spoke first, "Alas, the cases these past two days are mostly from poor and miserable people. There is no profit to be made!" At this time, the woman had just finished smoking a pipe and hurriedly drank a sip of hot tea. She made a gulping sound, and then exhaled a long breath, but the remaining smoke had disappeared. She said, "Ah, why should my lord bother himself! Like that opium case the day before yesterday, one case is worth several. How can we have that kind of fat meat every day?"

There was a finger-snapping sound outside the door. Then a servant walked into the room, standing in front of the bed with his hands at his sides, and reported to the man, "Reporting to the bureau chief: Someone outside reports that Wang Gongguan in a certain village is privately smoking opium. The reporter is waiting for the bureau chief to send a team to search and arrest them." The man smiled upon hearing this, and said, "Tell the chief inspector to catch them." As he spoke, he loaded another pipe and began to puff away. The servant responded and left.

After about half a cigarette time, the servant came in again and said, "The director of the Finance Bureau, the director of the Construction Bureau, and the director of the Education Bureau have come to visit." The man said "Please!" The servant went out and led the three guests in. The man and woman stood up at the same time. The man stepped forward and greeted them, "It's rare for the three of you to come together. What brings you here?"

"We're happy today, so we came to play eight rounds of mahjong with you!"

"Good, welcome!"

"..."

"...................."

After a round of greetings in different tones, the sound of dominoes dancing on the table could be heard. The woman was still standing by the man's side, watching their mahjong battle.

After two rounds of mahjong, the chief inspector returned. As soon as he entered the door, he smiled at the man and said, "The evidence in Wang Gongguan's opium case has already been secured, and we have also caught a gambling case and two private prostitutes in the vicinity!"

"The bureau chief's business is really good!" the three guests said in unison, praising him.

At about two o'clock in the morning, the mahjong game came to an end. The three guests were still not satisfied and insisted that the host accompany them to seek pleasure. The host, of course, readily agreed, and they set off together towards the pleasure quarters. Before they reached their destination, many prostitutes leaning against their doors saw them from afar and were so frightened that they retreated inside and closed their doors. When they went to knock on the door, a trembling voice inside answered, "We're not doing business anymore. Please spare us, lords!"

"Who said we're here to catch you? We're here to have fun!" the men outside said.

After a while, the door slowly opened. The lords walked in with smiles, finally restoring the frightened souls of the people inside!

The sound of singing, which had been absent from the air for a long time, was finally able to be revealed loudly tonight, as if it had received a special pardon.

Modern Psychology

A Glimpse of Road C 216

— Hu Yi

The click-clack of leather shoes echoed in the B Hotel; then, with a "whoosh," a modern girl wearing a fox fur stole, a coat, and high heels flashed out from the closing spring door. Before she had taken a step away from the door, a group of rickshaw pullers, as if they knew what was coming, were already waiting outside. Seeing that it was a superior girl, they became even more eager to solicit her. "Where to?" they all asked at the same time, scrambling to ask. "To W Lane on Road A." "Come on..." "How much?" "Is 300 cash okay?" Then they said 250 cash, even 200 cash."

Ha! Rickshaws were also having a big price cut.

One made up their mind and walked a few steps reluctantly.

Hello, Mister... I can't even shout over the noise, the welcoming sounds of "come, come, come" were singing in unison, and some were even patting the cushions, almost snatching her with their hands. I had never encountered such attentive rickshaw pullers before. It must be that they are particularly polite to women.

"Come on, you say..." "He also says come..." The rest also chimed in, "Hey! Come here!" The noise was so loud that she, who had just emerged from a moment of sweet pleasure, was of course not very clear-headed at the moment. Her brain seemed very tired, and her alluring eyes didn't seem able to lift their lids. How could she stand the loud clamor! With a huff, she said crisply, "I don't want it!" If I were to completely translate his original words, this strange national language must be his new invention. It was truly funny to hear, and I was confused by him. He had already guessed her intentions. The modern psychology, again, slanted her eyes toward her, pointed her hand to the seat, and made a ugly face that was neither smiling nor crying. Before the strange and bizarre show was over, she had already jumped into the rickshaw, pointed her hand in the direction of ×, and sped off in a puff of smoke.

Oh! So that's how business is done.

I sighed to the general despair of the rickshaw pullers and said, "The snipe and clam fight, the fisherman benefits. You guys were able to do it, and I really admire it." However, the quarreling rickshaws didn't seem to understand what I meant, and didn't express anything. I was also disappointed. Alas!
